Fierce Fighting Throughout Spain: Government Forces Send Large Reinforcements to the Sierra de Guadarrama; Rebels Use German and Italian Aircraft to Cover Preparations for Crossing the Sea 60

Madrid. Fierce fighting is taking place throughout Spain, and major developments are expected. It is anticipated here that a decisive battle may occur in the Guadarrama region north of Madrid in the next two days, as government forces have sent large reinforcements in an attempt to encircle the rebels, whose destination is Madrid. At the same time, rebel leader General Mola, while meeting with reporters in Burgos, the seat of the provisional government, said that although the navy had refused to join the revolution and the Basque Nationalist Party was fickle, all military operations were still proceeding according to the original plan. Mola also said that the revolutionary forces had transported a large part of their troops stationed in Morocco across the sea to Spain, and that these troops were now gradually advancing towards their destination, Madrid. He added that his troops in the north would certainly be able to make contact with General Franco's forces in the south. According to the rebels, after fierce fighting with the militias formed by local workers, they have occupied Ronda, located fifty miles northwest of Algeciras in southern Spain, with heavy casualties on both sides. It is also reported that Teruel, seventy miles northwest of Valencia, has also been occupied by the rebels. Judging from the current situation in Spain, it can be seen that the government controls Barcelona, the Mediterranean coast, and the inland provinces up to Malaga in the north, Madrid and its surrounding provinces, the Atlantic coast from San Sebastián to Oviedo, and a portion of the western border from Huelva northwards. The rebels now occupy Zaragoza and a large portion of the inland provinces, including the cities of Burgos, Valladolid, and Segovia. The southern end of Spain around Gibraltar, including Algeciras, the northwestern part of Spain around Corunna, and a portion of the territory along the Portuguese border. All Spanish colonies are in the hands of the rebels, with the government only having a foothold in the Balearic Islands. Therefore, judging from the above situation, the government now controls the industrial areas and the coastal areas, while the rebels occupy the agricultural provinces, but their access to the sea has been cut off except for the south and northwest. The rebels are now planning to unite their troops with the help of troops coming from Morocco. This morning, an aerial battle took place in the Strait, witnessed by a large number of people. It is said that as a result of the air battle, the government's air force gained a slight victory, with two rebel aircraft forced to descend and another two fleeing towards Ceuta in Spanish Morocco. (Reuters, 5th)

Ceuta, Spanish Morocco, North Africa. According to our correspondent, General Franco, commander-in-chief of the Spanish rebels, is now planning to send a large contingent of soldiers across the Strait of Gibraltar to return to the country and help in the war. If they are intercepted by warships belonging to the government forces, they will fight them. Currently, three postal ships are fully loaded with soldiers and weapons, ready to depart. At that time, six Italian aircraft, three German aircraft, and six other aircraft will escort them across the sea. These aircraft are ready for take-off at the air force base in Tetouan. The German cruiser "Deutschland" and the destroyer "Luchs" sailed to Cadiz in southern Spain yesterday. (Havas, 5th)

Areas Controlled by Both Armies: Southern and Northern Rebels Seek to Make Contact; Decisive Battle Seems Not Far Off 61

(Paris) Since the outbreak of the Spanish civil war, all war reports have been complex and confusing, and difficult to ascertain. Observers here have recently summarized the latest situation in both countries based on the most reliable information, namely that the rebel's attempt to occupy the capital Madrid and the government army's plan to recapture Zaragoza have both failed to materialize so far. The areas controlled by the government army and the rebel army are listed as follows:

(1) On the government army side, in addition to the capital Madrid and its surrounding areas, it still controls the following areas:

(a) The Extremadura region bordering Portugal in the southwest, including the provinces of Cáceres and Badajoz. (b) Most of the New Castile region in the center, including the provinces of Toledo and Cuenca. (c) The Murcia region along the Mediterranean coast in the southeast, including the provinces of Murcia and Albacete. (d) The province of Valencia. (e) A part of the province of Aragon. (f) The autonomous region of Catalonia, including the four provinces of Barcelona, Lleida, Tarragona, and Girona.

(2) The rebel army controls the following areas: (a) The entire Spanish Morocco in North Africa. (b) Most of the Andalusia region in the south, including the provinces of Seville, Córdoba, and Granada, although the province of Málaga is still in the hands of the government army. (c) An area in the southern part of the New Castile region. (d) The provinces of Galicia and León in the northwest, extending to the provinces of Valladolid and Segovia (northwest of the Sierra de Guadarrama). (e) The Old Castile region in the north, including the province of Burgos, where the "National Defense Junta" is located. (f) The province of Navarre in the north, from which the rebels plan to break out of Irún and San Sebastián to find access to the sea. (g) The province of Aragon, where the base of Zaragoza is located. (h) Three naval bases, namely (i) the port of Huelva, in the southwest, close to the Portuguese border, (ii) the port of Cadiz, along the Atlantic Ocean, northwest of the British port of Gibraltar, (iii) the port of Algeciras, near the port of Gibraltar. With the above situation now clear, it is possible to proceed to describe the general trend of the current war. Although the rebels hold three naval bases, all other ports on the Mediterranean coast are in the hands of the government army, and the navy is still loyal to the government. The rebels have had to change their original plan of operations, and are eager to find ways to enable the troops of General Mola, commander of the northern route, to make contact with the troops of General Trianu, commander of the southern route, so as to attack simultaneously from the north, southwest, and north, trapping the New Castile region in the center. As of now, the troops of General Mola, commander of the northern route, are waiting for the southern army to move north in large numbers to meet in the Central Plains, and are preparing everything. As soon as they occupy a good position, they will fight a decisive battle with the second government army. In recent days, fierce battles have taken place in the vicinity of the Somosierra Pass in the near north, the reason for which is precisely this. According to observers, the date for both sides to make a desperate gamble and decide the outcome is not far off, because both sides lack bullets, which is conducive to a quick battle. (Havas, 15th)

Conflicting War Reports from Both Sides: Claiming Progress on All Fronts 62

Madrid. The government has recently issued a war report as follows: (1) The General Staff has received a report from Colonel Sabia of the Northern Front, stating that his troops captured the village of San Rafael (north of the Guadarrama Mountains) last night, but did not occupy the village that night for fear of being attacked in the dark. (2) A column commanded by Lieutenant Colonel Mangada defeated a rebel team near Villacastín (on the way to Ávila) on the Northern Front yesterday. (3) Government forces in the province of Guadalajara (northeast of the province of Madrid) pursued the rebels and have crossed the city of Sigüenza in the northern part of the province. (4) Government forces have recently intercepted intelligence from rebel forces in various places, revealing that the rebel forces in Córdoba, Zaragoza, and Burgos are in dire straits due to a lack of ammunition. (5) The air force belonging to the province of Catalonia shot down an enemy aircraft east of Zaragoza. (Havas, 5th)

Burgos, Spain. A special dispatch from our correspondent, the "National Defense Junta" organized by the rebels, recently issued a war bulletin stating that the revolutionary forces on all fronts have made progress:

(1) In the Guadarrama Mountains on the Northern Front, although the aircraft belonging to the government forces are very active, the revolutionary army has made progress in its positions.

(2) The troops of General Franco, the leader of the revolutionary army on the Southern Front, have advanced towards the city of Madrid and occupied several positions, the names of which cannot be announced.

(3) In the villages of Azaila and Tardienta on the Eastern Front, southeast of Zaragoza, the revolutionary army of Zaragoza clashed with government forces, killing and wounding many and capturing many government vehicles.

(4) In the city of Cáceres on the Western Front (on the Portuguese border), after the revolutionary army clashed with government forces, the cities of Miajadas and Trujillo have been relieved. A total of ninety government troops were killed in this battle. In addition, the "National Defense Junta" strongly condemned the Madrid government's aircraft for dropping bombs on the port of Palma (on the island of Majorca in the Mediterranean) and the Cathedral of Our Lady in the cities of Huesca and Zaragoza, which have no defensive fortifications, as inhuman. It also stated that the aircraft bombing these places were not commonly used by the Spanish army, and that the bombs that fell on the ground were also different from the styles used in Spain, indicating that they were all from foreign countries. (Havas, 4th)

Government Air Force Bombs Rebel Base: Zaragoza in the North Is Strategically Important; Two Armies Are Deadlocked in the Mountains North of the Capital 63

Barcelona. The Cathedral of Our Lady in Zaragoza, which is currently stationed by a large contingent of rebel troops, is an important strategic location. It was bombed by aircraft belonging to the autonomous province of Catalonia, and it is reported that the rebels suffered extremely heavy losses. The government of the autonomous province has recently opened two new air bases in the provinces of Tarragona and Huesca to facilitate air force operations. The village of Azaila southeast of Zaragoza was captured by the rebels, but was immediately repelled by government forces by land and air, and the rebels suffered heavy losses, abandoning four field guns. In addition, according to news from the front line of the Guadarrama Mountains north of the capital, the government forces there have also made progress, having occupied the villages of San Rafael and Villardendre, north of the mountain pass. As for the front line in the province of Guipúzcoa in northwestern Spain, the rebels did not launch a counterattack as the government forces had expected. It is reported that the rebels are experiencing a severe shortage of supplies, especially a break in the source of gasoline, which has made them unable to move. (Havas, 4th)

Government Forces Capture Strategic Point North of the Capital 65

Madrid. The official confirmation of the government forces' recapture of the village of San Rafael north of the capital yesterday. The village is located northeast of the Guadarrama Mountains and is a popular tourist destination. It has been occupied by the rebels on the Northern Front since they started their revolt, because its terrain is dangerous and the roads from the capital north to the provinces of Segovia and Valladolid pass through the village, making it an important strategic hub. According to our correspondent, the column that captured the village was commanded by Colonel Sabia, bypassing the city of El Escorial west of the capital, circling down from the highest peak of the Guadarrama Mountains, surprising and attacking the rebels in the village of San Rafael, capturing it in one fell swoop, and entering the village that night, seizing a large number of firearms, ammunition, and cash. Our correspondent also went to the front line of the Somosierra Mountains in the north for inspection and sent a message saying that the rebels on that front fired a 155-millimeter cannon and threw incendiary bombs yesterday to cover two cavalry squadrons charging the government forces' positions. However, because the terrain there was not conducive to cavalry, and the government forces' defenses were solid, they immediately used machine guns to strafe the rebels when they saw the cavalry charging, annihilating all the rebels. At this point, the rebels no longer had the ability to launch an offensive. In addition, the rebel headquarters in the city of Burgos (i.e., the seat of the revolutionary army's "National Defense Junta") yesterday used wireless radio to direct the northern troops to recapture the village of Guadarrama with all their strength. Unexpectedly, this telegram was intercepted by the Ministry of the Army, which immediately notified General Li Gaiermei, the commander-in-chief of the Northern Front, to respond accordingly. The General decided to take preemptive action and sent two battalions of militias, namely the "Steel Army" Battalion and the "May 2nd" Battalion, to launch an offensive against the enemy's position, and ordered the artillery and air force to assist in the battle. A fierce battle will ensue. (Havas, 5th)

Pamplona, Spain. According to rebel sources, the Basque Nationalist Party and the Communist Party defending San Sebastián have now opened fire on each other, with heavy casualties on both sides. At the same time, the rebel headquarters in Burgos announced that it would not cede an inch of land occupied by the revolutionary army. It also said that the revolutionary army had made new progress in Guadarrama, the highlands of Madrid North, and that the enemy's aircraft had bombed them hard without effect. (Reuters, 5th)

Reuters Tokyo dispatch on the 2nd: Army Minister Count Terauchi declared that reform is what the nation needs today. Any cabinet member who cannot implement reform should resign immediately without hesitation. Politics is not my business, but I dare say that a cabinet member with a "weak knee" has no reason to remain in office. National reform naturally requires enormous funding. However, you do not need to raise taxes to raise it. Increasing taxes to raise 200 or 300 million yen is far from enough to meet the needs of our reform program. The urgent need now is to issue sufficient public bonds to cope with the current situation. The army's defense budget requires 300 million yen, but you should not be shocked by this. I will even go a step further and ask for 500 million yen. You should know that today's expenditures are not comparable to those of 30 years ago. In the past, defense expenditures were only calculated in tens of millions of yen, but now they must be calculated in hundreds of millions of yen. The country must strive to raise funds for national defense. If the expansion of national power is sought, the budget will continue to increase. If Parliament opposes the reform program, I will dissolve it, not just once, but again and again. We only seek to implement reform, regardless of the procedure.

Greece Declares Military Dictatorship; Dissolves Parliament and Declares Martial Law Throughout the Country; Resolves to Use Force to Stop Labor Strikes 75

Athens: An order for martial law throughout the country was issued here this morning, and the dissolution of the Greek Parliament and the establishment of a temporary dictatorial government by General Metaxas were announced. In his order, Metaxas stated that he ordered the dissolution of Parliament because it was unable to effectively sanction the systematic opposition to the government and the dangers of communist propaganda. If allowed to continue, it would lead to social and national misfortunes. This action by Metaxas follows the declaration of a general strike throughout Greece. The authorities are deeply concerned about the threat of a serious communist movement and have threatened to use force to end the strike, and have obtained the approval of King George of Greece to adopt this approach if necessary. (Fifth Reuters dispatch)

Athens: After King George II ordered the dissolution of the House of Representatives, Prime Minister Metaxas effectively became the dictator of Greece. He issued a proclamation to the people this morning, saying, "The situation is critical and cannot be dealt with without centralized power. I have been entrusted by the King with a heavy responsibility and will not hesitate to make every effort to save the country. I hereby inform the people of the country." Metaxas then explained the danger of communism and said that the distribution of seats in the current House of Representatives among the various parties was insufficient to produce a lasting government. This is why the King approved the two measures of promulgating martial law and dissolving the House of Representatives. "If any reactionary elements dare to undermine the Greek national revival movement, they will be severely punished without leniency." (Fifth Havas dispatch)

(London) According to Greek expatriates here, the main reason for the country's decision to establish a dictatorial government and dissolve Parliament is clearly because the communists in the House of Representatives have the power to hold the balance of power. Because the last election adopted a proportional representation system, the result was that the power of the Venizelos faction and the opposition party members in Parliament was almost equal. The Communist Party, because it won 15 seats, has a pivotal influence on the vote. The Greek expatriates here also said that because members of Parliament enjoy privileges, the Communist Party dares to cause disturbances without fear of being arrested. (Fifth Reuters dispatch)

Athens: The government recently promulgated new laws on labor issues, stipulating (1) that all labor-management disputes should be resolved through compulsory arbitration; (2) that minimum wage rates should be established; and (3) that labor insurance should be managed by the government. The left-wing labor unions are extremely dissatisfied with this law and have decided to hold a nationwide general strike from midnight today to express their protest, but the conservative labor unions do not agree. The situation is very serious at this time, and the government has ordered the police department to be cautious in preventing and maintaining public order. (Fourth Havas dispatch)

The US-German Trade War; Germany Issues New Measures to Retaliate Against the United States; Cancels the Use of Registered Marks to Pay for Goods 79

(Berlin) Banks here have received notification that an order will be issued tonight or tomorrow morning to cancel the method of using registered marks to pay for German exports. This step by the German side is clearly to retaliate against the United States' method of levying countervailing duties on German goods. Up to now, registered marks could be used to pay for certain types of goods, such as toys and pottery. It is said that half of the trade between Germany and the United States is paid in "aski" marks, 25% is paid in goods, and the remaining amount is paid in registered marks or part cash. After the issuance of this new order, the above-mentioned method will inevitably be completely overturned. At the same time, it is also reported that in the trade with the United States on Saturday and Sunday, the method of exchanging "aski" marks and goods was used. (Fourth Reuters dispatch)

(Washington) According to today's announcement by the authorities, the US Customs Bureau has issued new regulations requiring sellers of goods shipped from Germany to clearly state the amount of profit and the reason for exporting to the United States on the customs declaration form. At the same time, observers claim that the trade regulations recently issued by the German authorities are the result of learning that the German delegation stationed in Washington, D.C., announced that the current tariff war waged by the US Treasury Department cannot be reversed. (Fourth Reuters dispatch)

Former Acting Minister to Russia, Zhu Shaoyang, Subject of a Kidnapping Plot; Kidnappers Include Two Japanese and One Chinese; Mrs. Zhu Abducted; Police Intercept and Luckily Solve Case Immediately 95

Beiping Correspondence: Zhu Shaoyang, former minister to Finland and acting minister to Russia, has lived quietly in Beiping since retiring from his post, residing at No. 115 on the main street inside Chaoyangmen. He avoids politics, spending his time with poetry, books, and charitable endeavors. He currently serves as the vice president of the Mount Wutai Universal Relief Buddhist Association, going to the office every day. On the morning of the 4th, at around 8:00 AM, two Japanese and one Chinese, all wearing blue cloth gowns, arrived at the Zhu residence with cards, requesting to see him. Zhu's private car, number 四七三, was already parked in front of the gate, waiting to be used. They handed the cards to the chauffeur, which were imprinted with phrases such as "Entrusted by the Kwantung Army Headquarters," "Entrusted by the Military and Political Department of Manchukuo," and the name "Tada et al.," requesting to see General Zhu. The servant said this was Minister Zhu's residence, but they insisted on visiting Minister Zhu. They were led into the parlor and told that the minister was ill and could not receive guests, but the three repeatedly insisted. Zhu eventually came out, despite his illness, and after exchanging pleasantries, the three immediately said that two people, named Zhang and Li, whom the minister had criticized while in Finland, had now committed a crime. Therefore, the Gendarmerie Headquarters had sent them to ask the minister to come back and clarify the matter. Zhu said that was absolutely not the case. After repeated negotiations, nothing was resolved. Mrs. Zhu, Wang Jiawei, overheard the conversation indoors and reported it to the First District by telephone. The district immediately dispatched police officers to the Zhu residence. However, the three men brandished guns, drove the police into a room, and insisted on taking Zhu away. Mrs. Zhu volunteered to go in her husband's place, saying he was ill. The three then took her to the Zhu residence's private car, number 四七三, and drove west. After the three left, Zhu reported the incident to the municipal government by telephone. Mayor Qin Dechun ordered Counselor Zhu Ruilin to investigate together with Public Security Bureau Chief Chen Jigan and notified the Japanese police station to inquire about the situation. The Japanese side said they were unaware of the matter and dispatched personnel to investigate with our detectives. They learned that the car had left Xizhimen and was heading towards Changping County. They immediately notified the Changping County government to intercept the car. However, the car crashed into a ditch in Xisha Village, eight li from Changping, causing the car to overturn. The driver, Cao Defu, broke his leg, but the three men were unharmed. They took Mrs. Zhu and left. Cao went to Changping to report the case. It was already 2:30 PM. Soon, the county police arrived and captured two of the three men in a teahouse in Baifu Village near Xisha Village. After inspection, they were found not to be carrying guns. They were interrogated about the whereabouts of the others. They confessed that the others had taken Mrs. Zhu and villagers to Dongchu to take a car. The police immediately escorted the two men to Xisha Village, where they saw the other man holding a handgun and holding Mrs. Zhu. The man opened fire upon seeing the police, but luckily missed. He was captured by the police, and two handguns were found. Mrs. Zhu, Cao Defu, and others were escorted to the county. On the 5th, they will be transferred to Beiping. Beiping received the report of the solved case and learned that the men were staying at rooms 28 and 允 on Xiannmen Street, Xian Inn. Two were Japanese, named Kato Asaji and Ooyuu Eiichi. The Chinese man was named Ren Xiaoxia, also known as Yan Bowen, 26 years old, from Jilin. He had an 18-year-old mistress, Wang Shaoti, living with him. That evening at 7:00 PM, detectives went to Xian Inn to arrest them, but both rooms were empty. Inquiries at the inn revealed that all three men had a habit of taking white powder. They had left the inn at 10:00 PM on the 3rd and had not returned. Wang Shaoti had also left the inn on the morning of the 4th after receiving a phone call. While discussing the situation, another person came to the inn to inquire about the case, raising suspicion. He was arrested by the detectives. He confessed his name was Han Zixing, and he was taking white powder in a Korean opium den at No. 16 Houchang Alley. He was entrusted by Wang Shaoti to come and inquire about everything. Wang Shaoti was still taking white powder in the den. Detectives and police from the Fourth District went to Houchang Alley and captured Wang Shaoti. The cause of the incident has not been fully determined, but it is generally believed that the drug dealers failed to defraud money and resorted to kidnapping. (4th)

Banditry in Southwest Fujian Rampant; Investigation into Major Robberies in Recent Weeks; Pacification Headquarters Orders Divisions to Take Responsibility for Suppression 96

Xiamen Correspondence: The bandits in Southern Fujian and the Communist bandits in Western Fujian took advantage of the unrest in Guangdong and Guangxi to stir up trouble. Later, the largest bandit group, led by Zhang Kewu, was incorporated into the 11th Security Regiment and stationed in Datian. The six counties of Yongde, Dehua, Daquan, Putian, Xianyou, and Xintai in Southern Fujian gradually became peaceful. However, there was still a gang led by Lu Zhenshan entrenched in the second, third, and fourth districts of Anxi. The Security Office specially dispatched Adjutant Lin Qian to negotiate with them for incorporation. The negotiations have not been completed. Currently, banditry is still rampant in Anxi and Nan'an.

In Western Fujian, there are Communist bandits led by Zhang Dingcheng, and in Zhangpu and Nanjing in the Zhangzhou area, there are Communist bandits led by Zhang Changshui, all causing great harm. The following is a record of the most notable bandit activities in Nanquan and Zhangzhou and Western Fujian in recent weeks: (1) On the 21st, the bandit Guo Zong led over a hundred men to attack Pengxu, 30 li from Anxi city, burning several earth fortresses and looting over 100,000 yuan. Over thirty villagers, men and women, were killed. They retreated on the morning of the 22nd. (2) On the 23rd, Zhang Changshui led over a hundred bandits to intercept two passenger cars on the Longzhao Road at Makou Bridge in Zhangpu County. Fortunately, both cars sped through, but a soldier of the security escort team was killed and two passengers were injured. Later, they looted a cargo truck and burned it. The incident lasted for several hours. The large unit of the 75th Division rushed to the scene after hearing the news, and the bandits fled. (3) At 11:00 PM on the night of the 23rd, dozens of bandits attempted to attack the city outside the West Gate of Zhangping, but they were repelled by gunfire from the garrison. On the 25th, people from all walks of life in Zhangping telegraphed the Pacification Headquarters, saying, "Bandits are entrenched in the Wuliang and Erliang Mountains, burning, looting, and killing everywhere. They are dividing up the rice fields in the northwest second district and are now approaching the county seat several li away, posing an imminent danger. Please send troops to suppress them." It is reported that there are over a thousand bandits in the Wuliang Mountains. (4) On the 27th, a cargo truck on the Zhanglong Road carrying 3,000 jin of salt was attacked by bandits west of Shizhong. The driver was killed, and the salt was looted. This was the work of Zhang Dingcheng's gang. (5) On the 26th, a passenger car on the Longzhao Road from Zhangzhou to Zhangpu was attacked again by Zhang Changshui at Makou Bridge. Four soldiers from the 75th Division retaliated, and the bandits fled. (6) On the 27th, the town of Qilipu in Yunxiao was attacked by over five hundred bandits, who burned dozens of houses and looted everything. (7) On the 27th, the bandit Wu Wupengming led over a hundred men to attack Tanbian Village in Xiaoluoxi, Nan'an, looting over 20,000 yuan and kidnapping nine men and women, demanding a ransom of 5,000 yuan. (8) On the 28th, Wu Wupengming again attacked Putou Village in Xiaoluoxi, burning four houses, kidnapping ten people, and causing losses of several thousand yuan. (9) On the 29th, Zhang Changshui led over a hundred bandits to attack the villages of Yang, Piliao, and Qujiang in Nanjing County. The strong men's team came out to fight, but they were outnumbered. On the 30th, the villages of Zhangliao and Ban were also attacked. The bandits then attacked Fengqiaoping. The strong men retreated to Changjiao. At 9:00 PM on the night of the 30th, they continued to attack Kuikeng. Villagers in various villages who could barely support themselves were labeled as rich peasants. Currently, traffic from Shancheng to Chuanfan, Kuiyang, and Changjiao in Pinghe County is completely cut off. The organization "Military and Political Committee of the Chinese Soviet Republic of Southwest Fujian, Yonghe, and Jing" was discovered in the Changjiao, Youkeng, and Fengshuping areas of the third district of Nanjing. The fake chairman is Li Tianhui, and the fake vice-chairmen are Zeng Shouning and Luo Yongjian. (10) On August 1st, a passenger car on the Longzhao Road from Zhangpu to Zhangzhou was intercepted by dozens of Communist bandits at Gehoutaobiao, ten li from Liaopu County. The ticket seller, Deng Zishi, was killed and his body was abandoned by the roadside. The driver and all the passengers were kidnapped and disappeared.

The above only records attacks on towns and villages and interceptions of highways and cars. There are countless other sporadic bandit robberies. The Pacification Headquarters, due to the rampant banditry in Western Fujian and the Zhangzhou area, has specially ordered the 9th Division, 52nd Division, 3rd Division, and Independent 37th Brigade to take responsibility for suppressing the remaining bandits in Western Fujian. The 75th Division is responsible for suppressing the remaining bandits in the Zhangzhou area. The 75th Division's Han Brigade and various security regiments are responsible for suppression and appeasement in Anjing and Nan'an in the Quanzhou area. (August 2nd)

Major Construction Projects in Gansu Province; Focusing on Highways and Water Conservancy; Afforestation, Animal Husbandry, Cotton Planting, etc. Progressing Accordingly 97

Lanzhou Correspondence: Gansu Province has a vast territory, fertile fields, abundant resources, and thriving livestock. However, the population is sparse, development is delayed, and society is overly conservative, purely subject to natural environmental control. This has resulted in infinite resources being left to waste, which is a great pity. The provincial authorities are also facing financial difficulties and cannot do everything at once. They can only select key projects within the possible scope and try to develop them. First, highways and water conservancy are taken as the central work, and ways are sought to develop them. Afforestation, animal husbandry, cotton planting, cooperation, and other matters are also progressing easily. The general situation of the main construction work in recent years is recorded separately below:

Farmland Water Conservancy

Gansu Province has a high and dry terrain with little rainfall. Even in good years, the harvest is not enough to eat. In the event of drought, it is even more difficult for the people to make a living. According to surveys, the annual rainfall (referring to rain and snow) in the southern part of Gansu is 20 inches, and in the eastern part, it is 15 inches. The average annual rainfall in the province is at most 1.2 Chinese feet. In 1935 it was 1.1 Chinese feet. The actual water demand is at least 3 feet to be sufficient. It can be seen that even if Gansu is not droughty, the amount of water is still not enough. Although Xinjiang does not have much annual rainfall, we have not heard of drought, because the Altai and Tianshan mountain ranges, which are over 5,000 meters high, can store rain and snow. However, the mountains in Gansu Province are no more than 3,000 meters high, so they cannot store rain and snow. Currently, the total area of wasteland and cultivated land in the province is over 23 million mu, while there are only over 2.7 million mu of paddy fields. If the total population of the province, over 6 million, is divided equally, each person can only get half a mu. Each mu usually produces 400 jin of food per year, which is only enough to maintain the food supply for half a year for the entire province. The remedy is to increase the area of paddy fields by 3 million mu. However, Gansu is located in the upper reaches of the Yellow River, and the amount of water is relatively small. There are only 27 canals that can be opened along the Yellow River. When all are completed, a total of over 900,000 mu of land can be irrigated. In addition, wells must be dug on the plateau, or canals must be added to other rivers to increase the area of paddy fields by over 2 million mu, so that the people's food supply can be solved in drought years. The Taohui Canal project is currently being actively carried out by the Construction Department. The Tonghui, Shuifeng, and Xingu canals have also been surveyed one after another and are being designed. The Construction Department also borrowed 500,000 yuan from the Economic Commission, which will be used to excavate in rotation in the future.

Jailbreak in Putian; Thirty-Five Prisoners Escape on July 24th; Third Major Jailbreak in Just Nine Months 98

Xiamen Correspondence: A major jailbreak occurred at the Putian District Court Prison on July 24th. Thirty-five prisoners escaped. It has been investigated that there have been six or seven major jailbreaks in Putian Prison from last year to now. The largest was a major riot by prisoners on October 17th last year, when 61 people escaped. 19 were captured, and 42 escaped. The second major jailbreak was on June 17th this year, when 59 major criminals escaped. This is the third time. At 10:00 AM on the morning of July 24th, two prisoners from cell number three and two from cell number five were released to clean up the garbage in the yard, supervised by guard Chen. Unexpectedly, a prisoner from cell number five took advantage of Chen's inattention and struck him on the head with a stone. Chen immediately fainted. The four prisoners then opened the iron locks of other cells. Prisoners from several cells then surged out. Other guards came out to see what was happening and were immediately supervised, forced to open the locks of all the remaining cells, and released all the prisoners. They swarmed to the second prison gate, which had iron bars. The prisoners worked together to violently crash into the iron bars. The iron bars were not installed securely during construction and were knocked down. At that time, warden Deng Jimin was upstairs and fired two shots at the escaping prisoners in front of the door. The bullets hit the wall. The fifth trigger jammed, and the prisoners rushed to the main gate of the prison, broke the lock, and ran away in all directions. It was raining heavily at the time. Some of the prisoners had jailbreaking experience. Instead of escaping towards Tangbei Dingwei, they went in the opposite direction, calmly escaping into the crowded streets in front of the Tangxian Yamen. The county government heard the news and sent military police to pursue them. In the past, prisoners who escaped always fled towards Tangbei Dingwei, so the pursuit went in that direction. As a result, nothing was found. Of the 35 prisoners who escaped, including Yu Meihua, ten had been sentenced, two were military prisoners, and 23 had not been sentenced. (August 2nd)

Highway Transportation

The total length of the highways in Gansu Province is 7,000 kilometers. The main lines connecting to the outside are the Ganxin, Ganshan, Ganning, Ganqing, and Ganchuan highways. (There are two routes to Sichuan Province. The first route starts from Lanzhou, follows the Xilan Road to Huajialing, turns to Tianshui Cheng County Wudu, and connects to Guangyuan in northern Sichuan. The second route is from Lintan to Minxian, 50 kilometers long.) The construction cost is over 30 million yuan. The provincial authorities believe that the provincial treasury can hardly afford such a large amount, so for the construction of various highway projects, in addition to the old method of repairing bridges and culverts, earthwork engineering is completely done by requisitioning labor, so that the cost is low and the effect is great. The Ganshan Lanyao section, the Ganchuan Lantai section, and a part of the Tianma Road branch have been opened to traffic. The Lantao and Zhaoqin roads are partially completed. The Lanxiang section of the Ganqing Road is currently being actively rushed to repair. The Economic Commission's survey team led by Liu Rusong has surveyed the Ganxin Road to the first major section to Wuwei. It is currently organizing charts and will start construction as soon as it is completed.

Afforestation in Progress

Gansu Province has paid close attention to afforestation in recent years and has designated it as one of the most important construction policies. According to statistics, the number of trees planted each year was over 290,000 in 1933, over 400,000 in 1934, and over 1.5 million in 1935. The provincial government believes that mountain floods often occur in the summer and autumn seasons, causing disasters. If there are dense forests, the flood damage can be slightly reduced. Therefore, in order to expand the afforestation plan, it invited Fen Jueer, the deputy director of the Shaanxi Forestry Bureau, to Gansu for surveying last year. The Ministry of Industry also decided to jointly establish a forestry area in seven provinces, including Shaanxi, Gansu, Suiyuan, and Qinghai. A forestry bureau will be established as the competent authority for forestry affairs in each province and will carry out afforestation matters in stages. Afforestation along the Yellow River is also in progress. In addition, cooperation and animal husbandry are also being promoted separately according to the planned plans. However, Gansu's imports exceeded exports by over 23 million yuan last year. In the past, all income from opium was used to offset this, but now smoking is being gradually banned. The only remedy is to encourage cotton planting. It started last year, but there has been no significant effect. This year, 5 million jin of cotton seeds have been received and distributed to Gao and Yu counties for trial planting. If the expected results can be achieved in the future through cooperation between the government and the people, the trade deficit can be balanced.

Suzhou; Establishment of Running Water Underway 99

In previous years, local residents Xu Boming and overseas Chinese Liang and others initiated the establishment of running water to meet local needs. However, due to various reasons, it did not materialize. Recently, Shanghai merchants Wang Xiaolai, Shao Ruxin, and others initiated the establishment of running water together with local gentry Zhang Yipeng, Cheng Ganqing, and others. Several contacts have been made, and there are already some clues to the implementation plan. Yesterday, Shao Ruxin came to Suzhou from Shanghai to discuss the implementation with Cheng Ganqing and others. Shao then returned to Shanghai to discuss with Wang and others in order to realize it as soon as possible. It is reported that a preparatory office will be established in both Suzhou and Shanghai to facilitate contact. The share capital is assumed to be one million. The initiators in Shanghai will be responsible for 250,000, and the initiators in Suzhou will be responsible for 250,000. The Electric Power Plant has already recognized 50,000. There are 200,000 that will be raised by opening shares to the public. The water source may be taken from Lake Tai near Xukou, or from Cheng Lake in Yangcheng Lake, but it has not yet been determined. Once the contact is completed, the founders will be convened in Suzhou to hold an inaugural meeting and engage in preparations.

Smoked Meat Industry Strives for Tax Exemption 100

The Suzhou smoked meat industry previously requested the Chamber of Commerce to forward a request to the Ministry of Finance to strive for exemption from business tax, on the grounds that the industry had already paid slaughter tax. The request was disapproved. The Business Tax Bureau then sent personnel to collect business tax from various stores, resulting in misunderstandings. The shop assistant Chen Amao and others were arrested, but then released on bail. Now that the bureau must collect taxes in accordance with the regulations, the industry convened an extraordinary general meeting of member representatives from various stores on the 5th to discuss whether to pay business tax. As a result, based on the principle of one tax per item, they requested the Chamber of Commerce to forward the reasons to the Tax Bureau and the Department of Finance and strive for it in a reasoned manner to reduce the burden.

Wu Yannong's Estate in Litigation 101

Wu Yannong of Taohuawu in northern Suzhou was the richest man in Suzhou, with a huge fortune. Wu Yannong passed away ten years ago, leaving behind an estate of five to six million. Apart from a part that was divided among his children, most of the land was still managed by Wu Zishen of the second branch together with Wu Jiyu, a clan uncle. Now, Wu Silan of the sixth branch claims that his brother and others have not disclosed the management of the property for more than ten years and that there is a suspicion of embezzlement and fraud. He has specially hired lawyer Hu Shikang to write a complaint requesting the court to summon Wu Zishen and others to publicly announce the accounts for analysis. The District Court held a hearing on the morning of the 5th. The plaintiff was represented by lawyer Hu, and the defendant Wu Zishen also hired lawyer Jin Henian as his agent. Wu Jiyu hired lawyer Cai Taokang as his agent. After questioning by Judge Chen, it was decided to hold eight hearings.

Wuxi; Dispatch of District Instructors 102

The autumn sericulture season has already begun. The County's Sericulture Model Area Office held a departure guidance meeting at 8:00 AM yesterday in the area's auditorium. The meeting was attended by Director Long, the county magistrate, Deputy Director Zhou Yuanxun, and over a hundred district instructors. Chairman Zhou Yuanxun gave a speech, followed by a speech by County Magistrate Long and a speech by Cai Jingde. After the meeting, a photo was taken and the meeting adjourned. The instructors in the four townships and various districts departed uniformly on the 5th to establish guidance centers in various townships and prepare for all autumn sericulture guidance matters. However, due to budget cuts, ten fewer guidance centers will be set up in this autumn season compared to last year. There will be a total of 65 guidance centers in the county. A total of 90 instructors will be hired. There will also be two sericulture training classes with over 30 students. There have been some adjustments to the directors and instructors of the central guidance centers this term.

Jiading; Shanghai Steamboat Causes Death 103

The Jiangping steamboat of the Shanghai Gongmao Steamship Bureau was returning to Shanghai from Wuxi at 2:00 AM on July 31st. When passing the Dengjiajiao turn near Huangdu, it violently crashed into a rice boat belonging to Liu Ada of Wuxi. Boat hand A Bao was knocked into the river and drowned. A Da pursued the steamboat to Huangdu and reported it to the town's guard post, which detained the steamboat. Township Chief Zhang of Xihuang Township reported to the county government, which appointed Zheng Cheng, the head of the Nan Yi Public Security Branch, to lead officials to investigate. A Da and the steamboat crew were brought to the county for questioning. After questioning, it was clear that there was no way for Liu's boat to avoid the collision. The steamboat was still running at full speed at the turn. There was also no effort to rescue the victim after the accident. It was ruled that the Jiangping steamboat should compensate the deceased's family with 300 yuan to settle the matter.

Changshu; Thorough Investigation into Fish Tax Embezzlement 104

The fish tax collected at the Hupu fish market here during each fishing season is used to run local businesses. Recently, it was discovered that the fish tax collected by Yusheng Fish Bank in the area has not been remitted since 1927. Someone filed a complaint with the province. The Provincial Department of Finance, because the amount of the donation has been very large for ten years, sent a special investigator to Changshu, accompanied by the chief of the second section of the county government, to investigate. As a result, the historical account books of Yusheng, Futai, Yuda, Jutai, Longmao, and other five firms were brought to the county government for review to determine if there were any tax issues. However, because the various firms could not collect the historical account books in time, they were given seven days to send them to the county.

Zhenjiang; Damage to Jiaoshan Relics Case 105

The north of Jiaoshan has many rocks and strange shapes. Jiaodi Rock is one of the famous rocks in northern Jiaoshan. In the spring, the abbot of Dinghui Temple in Jiaoshan, Monk Jingyan, said that Xiaojiaoshan in northern Jiaoshan, which is dozens of square feet in circumference, could be used to build several houses to attract tourists. However, it is isolated in the river, dozens of feet away from the mountain. In winter, when the water is low, it is possible to walk back and forth. In summer, when the water is high, traffic is cut off. Jingyan decided to build a stone embankment to connect them. He had nowhere to take stone materials, thinking that there were many large stones on the northern slope of the mountain, so he bombed Jiaodi Rock to obtain the village. He did not know that it was Jiaodi Rock recorded in the mountain chronicle. Although there were people who warned him at the time, he did not pay attention. Then Xu Shanqing, a painter from Haiyun Temple who had lived on the mountain for a long time, came forward to sue Jingyan for intentionally destroying the relics at the court, county government, and county party headquarters. Before receiving the court's notice, Jingyan hired someone to salvage a larger stone that had been blown into the river. Fortunately, the three characters Jiaodi Rock were still on the stone. In fact, the old Jiaodi Rock was about two fathoms high and divided into two like horns. More than 20 people could sit on it, but the stone salvaged from the water was only as tall as a person, with no hills or valleys to speak of. Jingyan used this as evidence and asked the county government to issue a statement prohibiting anyone from suing him again. The plaintiff said that the size of the mountain stones was different before and after, and that the mountain was bombed for more than one day, which was known to everyone. The reasons for both parties were insisted upon, so they became deadlocked. Yao Qisu, a member of the county party headquarters, was sent to the mountain to investigate the truth of the case. He questioned both parties one by one and investigated the situation of the bombed stones. It has now been discovered and will be submitted to the county party headquarters meeting for discussion.

Danyang; Thousands of Acres of Farmland Flooded 106

The County has been raining for days. Mountain floods broke out. Thousands of acres of farmland in Houhu Township in the western countryside have been submerged. Yesterday morning, more than two hundred farmers, men and women, from the township braved the rain and entered the city to petition the county government and the first district office. Zhu Liquan, the township head, also submitted a petition requesting that relief be provided. In addition to telegraphing the county government, District Chief Zhang also sent a letter to Liu Yeqiu, director of the Lianhu Engineering Office, asking him to come to the office for consultation. As a result, Director Liu telegraphed the Jiangnan Water Conservancy Engineering Office to ask for instructions and was allowed to open the first and fourth gate of Lianhu West to discharge water. The engineering office then sent a letter to the first district office to check and handle it. District Chief Zhang then sent a letter to the Lianhu Property Management Office to open the gate to discharge water to save farmland. The farmers were satisfied and returned to their hometown.

Yangzhou; County Government Urges Payment of Land Tax 107

The county government believes that after the wheat harvest, new grains will soon be available, and the rural economy has seen a recovery. Jiaxing; Seedling Field Road Robbery Case 109

Zhu Hongquan, a bill collector from Yuansheng Rice Shop in Jia Yu Tanghui Town, collected 800 yuan in accounts from Chang'an, Xiashi and other places on the 4th, and took the night train back to Jiaxing. When he arrived at the station, it was already 8:00 PM. After getting off the train, he went to Mao Xinheng Transportation Company to rest, and then hired a rickshaw to return home. When passing the seedling field, two bandits suddenly appeared, holding wooden sticks, blocking the car from moving forward, and dragging Zhu out of the car, hitting him on the head with a wooden stick, causing Zhu to be injured and fall to the ground, losing consciousness. Two more bandits came and robbed all the 800 yuan in paper money and 17 yuan in hard currency from Zhu's body. After Zhu woke up, he tried to telegraph the Public Security Bureau. All the police officers were dispatched to search for the bandits in the area where the incident occurred, but the bandits had already gone far away. There have been no arrests until dawn. The reason for the robbery was that Zhu was checked by the police when he got off the car, and the paper money was exposed. The injured Zhu Hongquan went to Dexin Hospital for treatment that night.

Ningbo: Tax Police in Yao Seize Smuggled Salt 110

According to a secret report received by Shi Zutao, the supervising inspector of anti-smuggling stationed in Pingwang Town, Yao County, a large batch of smuggled salt was passing through the area. He immediately notified the 23rd squad of the local tax police and dispatched them to intercept and capture it. As expected, they seized ten large boats of smuggled salt, weighing over 50,000 catties, in a small river ditch near Ditang. At the time, the smugglers, relying on their numbers, dared to open fire and resist. The tax police surrounded them on three sides and launched a fierce counterattack. The smugglers were no match and fled. Except for one smuggler who was shot and wounded on the spot, the rest were taken back to the team for interrogation and transferred to the local court for trial.

After the passing of Mr. Wu Xingya, Central Executive Committee Member of the Chinese Kuomintang, Standing Committee Member of the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee, and Director of the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau, due to illness in Guling at 9:30 PM the night before last, Mayor Wu Tiecheng sent a telegram of condolence yesterday and immediately appointed Education Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan as concurrent acting director, to take office this morning. Passed Away the Night Before Last

Mr. Wu Xingya followed the Premier and served the Party and the country, making outstanding contributions. In February of this year, he suddenly suffered a stroke at his residence in Shanghai. He was examined by two doctors, Jia Dingna and Laiman, and gradually recovered. On the 5th of last month, he followed the doctor's advice and took his family to No. 225 Poyang Road, Guling, for convalescence, and sent a caregiver along. As for bureau affairs, Secretary Li Suixian acted on his behalf. On the 3rd, the old illness relapsed and worsened. He telegraphed doctors Jia Dingna and Laiman in Shanghai to fly to Lushan for consultation, but the condition had already entered a coma, making it impossible to provide treatment. He passed away at 9:30 PM on the 4th.

After receiving the bad news, Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng ordered all municipal government agencies to fly flags at half-mast to express mourning and sent a telegram of condolence, which read: "To Wu Li Qiwen at No. 225 Poyang Road, Guling, I was shocked to hear of the sudden death of my brother Xingya. I am deeply saddened. I hope you will restrain your grief and take care of the important matters. I send my condolences." At the same time, considering the importance of the position of Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, he immediately appointed Education Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan as concurrent acting director and convened a meeting with Wu Kaixian, supervisory committee member of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Education Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan, Public Security Bureau Director Cai Jingjun, and Secretary-General Yu Hongjun to discuss the preparations for the memorial service.

Preparing for Memorial Service

The original telegrams and eulogy are recorded below.

Two Telegrams of Condolence

In addition to ordering all levels of party headquarters to lower flags and comrades throughout the city to wear gauze to express our grief, we have specially sent Committee Member Jiang Huaizu to fly to Lushan to pay respects. The pillar has collapsed, and I am extremely saddened. I respectfully send my condolences and hope you will restrain your grief. Wu Kaixian respectfully, printed seal."

Party Headquarters Eulogy

"On this sixth day of August in the twenty-fifth year of the Republic of China, the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang and all working comrades respectfully offer incense and flowers to the spirit of Mr. Wu Xingya, Standing Committee Member, and say: Alas, Mr. Wu, a hero of our Party, born of the spirit and beauty of the Jing Mountains and the E River, a brilliant figure, a pioneer for the people, embracing the doctrine, following the Three Principles of the People, dedicating himself to the Party and the country, joining the army with his pen, assisting the revolution, and achieving success. When he opened the government in Anhui, he left behind a legacy of care. When he moved to Shanghai, he benefited farmers and workers. Leading comrades, he remained loyal. All looked up to him, and the masses admired him. The central government relied on him, and his virtue was rising. But heaven did not bless him, and he suffered an untimely death. The two evil spirits raged, attacking his body. He went far to Guling to recuperate in the Lushan mountains. Medicine was ineffective, and he traveled long to the realm of immortals. The news came like a thunderbolt in the clear sky. Citizens shed tears of snow, and comrades beat their chests. Alas, how vast is the blue sky, how dreamlike is this dream. Your crane carriage has flown far away, but your voice and appearance are still here. A bunch of incense and flowers, a cup full of clear wine, we offer a sorrowful tribute by your coffin, choked with endless regret. May your spirit come and accept this sincere sorrow. Alas, may you enjoy this!"

Mr. Wu's Biography

Mr. Wu was 46 years old, from Huangmei County, Hubei Province, and resided at No. 60 Shanzhong Road, Shanghai. He had one wife, two sons, one seven years old and the other three years old, and three daughters. His eldest daughter is married to Sun Yuanliang, the current commander of the 88th Division of the Central Army, as his wife. The second daughter is nine years old, and the youngest is eight years old. When Mr. Wu went to Lushan earlier, they all accompanied him. In his early years, Mr. Wu deeply lamented the corruption of the Manchu Qing government and joined the revolutionary party as a member. He served by the Premier's side during the uprising at Bai'etan. After the Premier passed away in Beijing, Mr. Wu followed Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek. During the Northern Expedition in the 15th year of the Republic of China, he served as the confidential secretary of the General Headquarters of the National Revolutionary Army, the secretary of the Special Party Department of the General Headquarters, the director of the Political Department of the 37th Army, the director of the Civil Affairs Department of the Anhui Provincial Government, the acting chairman, and the director of the Civil Affairs Department of the Hubei Provincial Government. He is currently a member of the 5th Central Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang, a standing committee member of the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee, and the director of the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau. Mr. Wu participated in the revolutionary work for more than 20 years and was highly valued by Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek. Now, he suddenly passed away due to a stroke, and all of Mr. Wu's friends are mourning his loss.

Telegram from the Labor Movement Association

The Shanghai Labor Movement Students Association sent a telegram of condolence to Mr. Wu's family because Mr. Wu had served as the director of the Labor Movement Personnel Training Institute and was a sponsor of the association, with whom they had a particularly close relationship. The original telegram is recorded below: "To Mrs. Wu, Upon reading the newspaper, we were shocked to learn that Mr. Wu passed away suddenly due to a stroke. The bad news has arrived, and we are deeply saddened. Mr. Wu was a distinguished elder of the Party and the country, a model for the youth, who worked tirelessly for the revolution and made outstanding contributions. At this time of national crisis, when Mr. Wu should have been taking on difficult tasks, heaven did not bless us and took away our virtuous man. In addition to shock and grief, we are deeply saddened. We hope you will restrain your grief and take care of yourself to carry on Mr. Wu's wishes. Respectfully, the Shanghai Labor Movement Students Association."

Explanation of National Assembly Election Regulations Should Be Submitted to the Election Authority First 113

The Shanghai National Assembly Representative Election Office received Order No. 8 of the Minguo General Division from the Nanjing National Assembly Election General Office yesterday, which reads: "In order to comply with the order, it has recently been found that people in various places believe that the power to interpret the National Assembly Representative Election Law and the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the National Assembly Representative Election Law belongs to this office. They are submitting requests for interpretation to this office. After review, some have already been clearly stipulated, and some are factual issues. If we answer each case, it will not only easily cause disagreements but also be time-consuming. In the future, if people or groups in each election district have any matters for which they request interpretation of election laws and regulations, they should submit them to the election authority in charge for review. If it is deemed to be a question of interpretation, it should be forwarded to this office immediately. Otherwise, it should be approved and issued directly to save procedures. It is hereby ordered that the office comply with this order and forward it to the people in the area under its jurisdiction for their information." It is also heard that the office has also received a similar official letter from the General Supervisor of the Election of Free Professional Groups and has already complied with it and forwarded it. The Changde steamer of the Leping Steamship Company disappeared outside Shantou port for many days. There were more than 600 passengers and more than 70 crew members on board. All parties concerned were very anxious about this. Northeast Woolen Fabric Transit Tax Should Be Changed to Import Tax; Municipal Chamber of Commerce Submits Request to Ministry of Finance 121

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance yesterday: "For the matter of submitting a request, on the 4th of this month, according to a letter from the Shanghai Woolen Fabric Industry Association, the issue of inspection and anti-smuggling has been actively carried out by the inspection and anti-smuggling committee organized by your association. The association has been complying with the measures to prevent and eliminate smuggled goods. However, it has been found that the transit goods of Shanhaiguan woolen fabric, also known as ABC, which are not smuggled goods, are more serious than smuggling. After paying the ex-factory tax in the three eastern provinces, they can be transferred to the mainland with a joint transport bill. According to its tax rate, only 7.5% is paid for every 100 yuan of value, compared with the import tax of 45% for every 100 yuan, the difference is as much as 37.5%. Therefore, all products not produced by the factory can be transferred from Shanhaiguan under the name, and the tax rate can be reduced by the ex-factory tax, and they are treated the same as regular goods, and can be transported unhindered. The cost of goods is reduced, and the selling price is cheaper. The goods are tax-paid, and there is no way to prevent them. They affect the national regular tax and disrupt the commercial market. Its disadvantages are even more serious than smuggling. Furthermore, it has been found that the original ABC only refers to two kinds of woolen fabrics, but now there are many colors. Woolen fabrics have everything. The number of products is increasing day by day. If this continues, all manufactured products can be transferred at will, endlessly. The harm is immeasurable. The association is now afraid and trembling. However, this matter is important. It is not possible to correct the root cause without a comprehensive plan and countermeasures. For this reason, we are writing to request your association to forward it to the government for fundamental design and clarification of measures to maintain tax revenue and stabilize commerce, etc. The association checked the woolen fabrics. If they are made in the three eastern provinces and transported into Guan for sale through Shanhaiguan, in principle, they should be regarded as transit goods and only transit tax should be levied. However, under special circumstances in the three provinces, it is not possible for us to audit whether they are actually manufactured locally or whether there is any concealment. If we adhere to the text and meaning, it is enough for large-scale dumping. Therefore, after the closure of the customs of the three eastern provinces, during the relocation of taxation, the goods from the three eastern provinces, in addition to the few kinds designated by your department, which are definitely produced in the three eastern provinces and have no similar products, are still recognized as transit goods and transit tax is levied. All others are levied import tax according to the import tax regulations. This matter is consistent with the regulations and has a precedent to follow. Therefore, it is reasonable to report to your department for verification. Your department should carefully review the above-mentioned precedents and strictly restrict them, so that the national tax revenue and industrial and commercial livelihood can be preserved.
