Selling Artificial Silk Fabrics: Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Petitions for Certification by Guilds 124

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday submitted a petition to the Ministry of Finance, stating: "Regarding the matter of submitting a truthful report: On the 3rd of this month, the Shanghai Silk Fabric Trade Association wrote to us, stating that, in order to assist the government in preventing smuggling and to protect the sale of legitimate goods, and in accordance with the 'Provisional Regulations for Investigating the Transportation and Sale of Imported Goods' promulgated by the Ministry of Finance, as well as the 'General Rules for Investigating Smuggling by Various Industries' of the Inspection and Anti-Smuggling Committee of your association, the Silk Fabric Inspection and Anti-Smuggling Committee was established. After several discussions by the association's Executive Committee, fifteen inspection rules, a voluntary registration form, an application form, and other relevant documents were formulated. A resolution was passed at the extraordinary meeting of member representatives on July 31 to set August 2nd to 11th as the registration period for existing stock. Currently, the association is supervising its various groups to implement the regulations in accordance with the inspection rules. In accordance with Articles 6 and 7 of the 'Provisional Regulations for Investigating the Transportation and Sale of Imported Goods' of the Ministry of Finance, when imported goods are transported to different locations, they can be accompanied by a delayed sales certificate issued by the Customs and a distribution form issued by the trade association. However, Articles 4 and 6 of the 'Measures for Investigating and Clearing Domestically Produced Piece Goods Made of Artificial Silk' stipulate that domestically produced piece goods made of artificial silk must obtain a transportation and sales permit from the Customs. This means that imported artificial silk can be transported and sold without hindrance by simply obtaining a distribution form from the trade association, while domestically produced piece goods made of artificial silk must obtain a transportation and sales permit from the Customs for each batch. This is a reversal of priorities and an inconsistency in difficulty. We respectfully present the situation of our industry and our humble opinions as follows: (1) Silk fabrics are mostly sold by traders through multiple channels, not directly by manufacturers to various locations. Silk fabric traders cannot provide artificial silk tax receipts and can only present invoices from the selling merchants and certificates from the inspection and anti-smuggling organizations in the production areas. (2) Silk fabric sales always start from a single bolt. Requiring a transportation and sales permit from the Customs for each bolt would cause inconvenience to both officials and merchants. (3) The fifteen inspection rules established by the association include registering existing stock and materials, stamping each item to trace the origin, and registering new stock and materials, requiring verification of tax payment certificates and supporting documents. Furthermore, a re-inspection is required before transportation and sale, and certificates are issued upon verification, which is comprehensive and prevents any loopholes. The procedures are already extremely cumbersome. If we were to follow the above-mentioned 'Measures for Investigating and Clearing Domestically Produced Piece Goods Made of Artificial Silk,' then the hundreds of silk stores in the city would be transporting and selling thousands of bolts of silk fabrics daily, and requiring a permit from the Customs for each bolt would be time-consuming and uneconomical. Furthermore, the store staff would not be sufficient to handle the workload, and the running around and congestion would be unbearable. Therefore, we request your association to forward this matter to the Ministry of Finance, so that the transportation and sale of imported artificial silk and imported artificial silk fabrics should be handled in accordance with the 'Provisional Regulations for Investigating the Transportation and Sale of Imported Goods' promulgated by the Ministry of Finance. As for domestically produced piece goods made of artificial silk and blended silk, we request that the association's inspection rules be followed. After the association verifies and issues certificates, transportation and sale should be permitted in order to maintain legitimate commerce and reduce unnecessary procedures." Upon consideration, silk fabrics produced by silk weaving factories are mostly sold through traders, not directly. Therefore, it is possible for silk weaving factories to obtain tax payment evidence from artificial silk import merchants in exchange for a transportation and sales permit. However, it is practically impossible for silk fabric traders to require silk weaving factories to provide evidence of artificial silk import tax payment for each batch before purchasing. Furthermore, there is no legal basis for obtaining transportation and sales permits from the Customs based solely on the invoices issued by silk weaving factories. It is difficult to approve this request, as it is the most challenging issue currently faced by traders. The key to whether tax-evading artificial silk is used as raw material lies with the weaving factories. Now that nine articles have been established to strictly regulate and restrict these weaving factories, domestically produced silk fabrics should not contain any mixed use of tax-evading raw materials. Therefore, a simpler and easier method can be devised for auditing traders. Furthermore, Articles 4 and 6 of the aforementioned inspection and clearing measures specifically refer to factories and do not include traders. Therefore, the association's request for the association to issue certificates for the sale of domestically produced artificial silk fabrics does not seem to contradict the original regulations. We have enclosed the certificate form, voluntary registration form, and inspection rules formulated by the association and respectfully submit this report to your department for review and approval. Implementation would be a matter of public convenience.

Tonghua Steamer Bravely Sails to Wodou: Place Name Not Listed on Charts or Maps; Loaded Salt and Returned to Fujian, Daring Not to Go Again 125

Shaopu, also known as Wodou, opposite Shantou port, is a place of extremely abundant sea salt production. However, because the islands are dense and the reefs are numerous, there has never been a navigable route. The place name is not listed on any sea charts or maps. Now the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Tonghua steamer has decided to sail there, taking a great risk and sailing on a non-scheduled route. The events it experienced are quite interesting and worthy of reporting.

Old Man as Pilot

Shaopu is located inside Wodou, surrounded by islands and reefs. The local people usually make a living by drying sea salt. Men and women are unusually brave and armed, each equipped with small boats, appearing and disappearing on the nearby sea surface, regarding the looting of merchant ships as a business. Civilian boats in the Shantou and Fujian area warn each other not to sail there. This time, the Tonghua steamer sailed there to load 100,000 dan of sea salt to Fujian. However, because the place is not listed on any sea charts, navigation was extremely dangerous. Special efforts were made to hire a pilot familiar with the harbor there, who was over seventy years old. He was first asked to sail from Shaopu in a small boat to the sea surface and then transfer to the steamer to guide the Tonghua to Wodou and drop anchor. When the pilot arrived on the Tonghua, he said to the crew members: "Wodou and Shaopu have not seen an ocean-going ship for many years. I am fortunate to be able to board an ocean-going ship as a pilot."

Bandits Attempt to Loot

The salt farmers in that area are actually bandits. They have always made a living by plundering civilian boats. Now, seeing the Tonghua steamer arrive at Wodou, they attempted to rob it. However, the Tonghua steamer also knew that the place was a den of bandits. The salt affairs inspection office had sent a squad of water police in advance, carrying firearms, to protect the ship. After the Tonghua arrived, the island bandits immediately divided into twelve small boats, each boat with more than ten people, holding sharp weapons. They arrived late at night, surrounded the Tonghua, and tried to climb aboard to rob it. The first time, the water police opened fire, and the bandits could not get close to the ship and fled. The second time, they came with even greater force and fought with the water police for a long time. Although the bandits were repelled, the water police squad leader was frightened and became ill.

Safe Return to Fujian

The sea salt produced in that area is very black in color and extremely unattractive. The value is extremely low. One national currency yuan can buy 2,000 jin or 3,000 jin. This is because things are cheap when there is a lot of them. After the Tonghua steamer risked going to load 100,000 dan, the price of salt in that area immediately increased to one yuan to buy only 800 jin. After the Tonghua steamer transported the salt to Fujian, it no longer dared to risk sailing there.

Ningbo Association in Shanghai Cables: Urgently Seeking a Solution to the Daishan Tragedy; Need to Improve Harsh and Hasty Practices; Poor Implementation by Lower-Level Organizations 126

The Ningbo Association in Shanghai yesterday sent a cable to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, the Salt Affairs Bureau, the Zhejiang Provincial Government, and the Liangzhe Salt Transport Commissioner's Office regarding the Daishan tragedy, stating: "Regarding this unfortunate incident in Daishan, our association has received reports from our fellow villagers in Daishan, informing us that the greed and recklessness of the tax police stationed in Daishan were the main reasons for inciting the incident. Fortunately, the Yinxian District Administrative Commissioner rushed to quell the situation, appease the refugees, and assign the responsibility for arresting the murderers to the local officials, preventing the tax police from taking the opportunity to retaliate and extort money. The handling was essential, and the situation in the area has been temporarily stabilized. However, after the pain subsides and we reflect on this unprecedented tragedy, we must urgently seek a solution. We believe that the crux of the matter is that the recent handling of fisheries and salt affairs by the salt affairs organizations has been too harsh and hasty, and there is a need for improvement. Based on what our colleagues know, there are several points that we will briefly describe as follows:

Fishing Surveillance Changes

While still in the research stage, Rongcheng County in Shandong Province has been approved to temporarily exempt fisheries and salt from implementation in order to prevent disputes. However, Daishan has not yet been approved. Tax police arbitrarily demand things, and if things are not done according to their standards, they are punished. Fishery salt confiscated due to discoloration is resold by the tax police without waiting for it to be dyed. The salt farmers witness this and become increasingly resentful. Furthermore, discolored salt, regardless of whether it is red or black, cannot be welcomed by customers for pickling fish. Using rice bran will cause it to rot due to heating. It is recommended that the current method be immediately stopped and that it be implemented after the experiment is improved or after adopting regulations from neighboring countries in order to avoid unnecessary sacrifices. This is the first point.

Selling Fish Surveillance

There has never been a time limit because offshore fishing tides are extremely important. Occasionally missing the right time will result in wasted effort. In the old system, regardless of the time, even late at night, salt could be purchased and the anchor could be raised. Now, time is limited from 9:00 AM to 4:00 PM. No flexibility is allowed after the time limit, resulting in fishermen having orders but no salt, missing the fishing season, and suffering unexpected losses. It is recommended that orders be issued to restore the old regulations in order to show compassion. This is the second point.

Fishing Surveillance Order

Previously, it was only once a year, then changed to once a season. Now, an order must be obtained for each trip to sea, which increases the tax by five to six times compared to the initial annual order. Furthermore, any salt left over from the previous order must be confiscated. Fishermen do not catch much fish, resulting in salt being left over. The old regulations allowed them to temporarily store it and take it back on the next trip to sea, which was a fairer approach. It is recommended that the issuance of orders be relaxed appropriately and that strict orders be given not to confiscate leftover salt in order to slightly reduce the burden on fishermen. This is the third point. Handling old piles of salt has already caused inconvenience to salt farmers, and the failure to provide timely compensation for the use of civilian land has led to widespread resentment and rumors. It is said that salt farmers make a living by drying salt, and in good years, they are only self-sufficient. They are deeply afraid that transporting salt back will waste working time and that the reduction in production will affect their lives in the future. This is their actual situation of fear. Those whose salt fields have been enclosed and cannot continue to work have even greater resentment. It is recommended that efforts be made to avoid the suffering of salt farmers and that compensation be paid on time for the enclosed salt fields so that unemployed salt farmers can find alternative livelihoods. This is the fourth point. In short,

Government Affairs Should Maintain the Big Picture

It is not appropriate to be overly demanding in everything. What is being done now has the opposite effect. The Daishan incident has already happened. In addition, tax police in Shenjiamen are known for deducting salt from farmers' labor (farmers transport saline mud to pay for labor, which is called labor salt), and tax police in Ningbo are known for dumping the old salt from fish shops (wooden buckets used to hold pickled fish have leftover salt, and salt police order them to be dumped and not reused, resulting in repeated conflicts). All the demands are extremely trivial, resulting in insufficient revenue and excessive harassment of the people. This may not be entirely the intention of the salt affairs authorities, but rather due to poor implementation by lower-level organizations. In the old system, tax police who suppressed smuggling were controlled by nearby bureaus, and the bureaus had the right to correct any excessive harassment of the people. Now, the tax police stationed in a part of the area are allowed to exercise their powers freely. If the leader is incompetent or if they are eager to claim credit, the harm that they can cause is unimaginable. This is another issue that should be discussed in the current system. Lao Tzu said, "The people do not fear death, why threaten them with death?" The people have never not feared death, but when forced to die, they do not fear it. When they do not fear death, there is nothing they cannot do. The outbreak of the Daishan case is frightening. Now that there are many border troubles, these people who are accustomed to wind and waves and are physically strong, and the public should be especially taken care of by the government. Our association has a connection to our hometown, and we have seen what has happened. We dare not fail to report it in detail. We hope that you will pay attention to it and await your orders.

We are eagerly awaiting orders. Respectfully submitted.

Xu Deyu's Nephew Abducts and Conceals His Young Child 136

Xu Deyu, a Yangzhou native who runs an inn at 67 Zhou Shan Road, has a six-year-old son named Kou Dingzi. The day before yesterday afternoon around 2 PM, Xu's nephew, Huo Weicai (age 18), took him out, ostensibly to Huishan Road to buy sugarcane scrapings. However, he conspired with Liu Shuzhi, a Jiangbei native living at 7 Bei Kai Er Road, to abduct the child. Liu took the child to live at the home of Dong Agui, a local resident at 235 Pingliang Road, intending to sell him for profit. After the incident was reported, the Huishan Concession police dispatched Chinese detective Zhao Yongqing to arrest Huo, Liu, and Dong. The child, Xu Kou Dingzi, was rescued and taken to the police station. The father retrieved the child. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Zhang Shizhu, a miscellaneous worker from the Public Works Department, explained the situation and requested prosecution. Subsequently, the victim Xu Deyu brought his son to testify to the events. When questioned, Huo and Liu stammered in their testimonies. Dong Agui claimed that Liu Shuzhi came with the child, saying he was just waiting for his brother to pick him up and that he was unaware of the abduction, pleading for leniency. Judge Xiao Bianfen sentenced Liu Shuzhi to one year and two months of imprisonment, and Huo Weicai to ten months. Before execution, they were ordered to undergo six months of reformatory education at a reformatory. Dong Agui was released.

Japanese Sailor Case Continues Investigation for Evidence - Old Man Yang Zengquan and Three Others Testify in Court Yesterday - Yang Wendao's Palm Print and Rust Inside Book Still Need to Be Analyzed - Ye Haisheng and Yang Wendao Both Wept Bitterly Yesterday 137

The three suspects in the murder case of Japanese sailor Nakayama Hideo, Yang Wendao, Ye Haisheng, and Zhou Sherong, were escorted by the police to the First Special District Court yesterday afternoon at 2 PM. Judge Xiao Xiefen specially opened the First Court to continue the investigation. Prosecutor Tang Peiyou and Clerk Ding Chongnan were also present. The Public Works Department's prosecuting lawyers Bo Liang, Ru Bao Yi, and Li Zhishan, as well as the defendants' defense lawyers Zhang Zhitian, Fan Gang, Tang Huaiqun, Wang Shizong, and Guo Qiming, all appeared in court. The Municipal Government and the Public Security Bureau also sent Secretary Zhang Tingrong and Section Chief Huang Hua to observe the proceedings.

More than ten members of the Japanese army stationed in Shanghai

were present to observe. This was the second court hearing after the closure of the debate in the case. Since it was still a continuation of the investigation for evidence, there was no need for a special collegial panel. Therefore, Judge Xiao investigated the case independently. First, Lawyer Ru stated that Yang Jianzhong, whom the defendant Yang Wendao had implicated in the frame-up, had been repeatedly investigated by the police, but his whereabouts could not be found, so he could not be summoned to court for questioning. The police originally did not need him to testify. Since Yang Wendao

was framed by him,

he should bear the responsibility of providing evidence and finding Jianzhong. In addition, four witnesses who should be summoned have now been gathered. Judge Xiao immediately ordered Clerk Ding to read aloud the transcript of the visit to the scene of the incident on Doule'an Road by the witness Pan Qiaoying, a woman who was summoned from Gaoyou on the 28th of last month at 9 PM by the police and lawyers, during which Pan performed the situation of witnessing the murderer shooting down Nakayama Hideo. Then, he asked the three defendants about their

opinions on Pan's

statement. Yang and Zhou both shook their heads and said they had none. Ye claimed that Pan went into the stove shop after hearing the gunshot and could not have seen the murderer's appearance. Judge Xiao then explained in detail the reason why the originally scheduled continuation of the court hearing on the 31st of last month was not held as scheduled. He said that since the closure of the debate in the case, it was necessary to investigate and summon witnesses, so the hearing was scheduled for the afternoon of the 31st of last month. However, since the witness Pan Qiaoying, who was summoned from Gaoyou, had been

summoned to Shanghai

on the 27th and she could not wait, the hearing was advanced to the 28th for questioning about everything. After the questioning was completed, the scheduled date of the 31st could be cancelled. However, there were misunderstandings due to external rumors that did not know the truth. It should be known that the case is still in the process of investigating evidence. Also, the four witnesses summoned must be questioned separately, and many of the questions were related to Yang Wendao. Therefore, he ordered the bailiff to take Yang and the four witnesses out of the courtroom before questioning them one by one. First,

the seventy-three-year-old

old man Yang Zengquan was brought to the court and stated that his ancestral home was Zhongshan, Guangdong. He was engaged in printing in Shanghai and had an uncle-nephew relationship with Wendao. The Beishan Yang Clan Shanghai Association was established by the clansmen in Shanghai for more than ten years. The court immediately showed him two letters from the association to Wendao found in Wendao's home and questioned him about the matters mentioned in the two letters. After reading the letters, Zengquan said that the two letters were sent by the members after Wendao returned to his hometown last year because they learned that some clansmen had stolen public property. Therefore, they sent the letters to Wendao, asking him to stop them nearby. Although he was

the president of the association

at that time, he only knew the general situation of the matter. If detailed information was needed, please ask Yang Haichou. Subsequently, Yang Haichou, who was in his seventies, testified that he and Wendao were also distant uncle-nephews. In the past, because a certain clan chief in his hometown acted like a local tyrant, running rampant in the village and oppressing the people, and had more than ten henchmen under his command, he privately sold public land last year. The clansmen sent a letter asking for help. Wendao returned to his hometown, so the association sent a letter to Wendao, asking him to overthrow the clan chief. Because Wendao

had been away from his hometown for a long time,

they nominated seven good people in the village to assist him. The "help" mentioned in the letter refers to helping Wendao overthrow the clan chief, and the so-called "killing this scoundrel" also refers to dealing with the clan chief. He is currently imprisoned in Zhongshan County, etc. Yang Huiji, the secretary of the association, and Yang Junyi, a member, also came to court to testify that the purpose of the two letters sent by the association to Wendao was purely to ask him to work with the other seven people in his hometown to deal with the local tyrant and

maintain public property,

and there was no other purpose, etc. When questioned, the defendant Yang Wendao's statement regarding the letter was similar to that of the four witnesses. He also stated that he decided to return to Guangdong to send his uncle home. The court then read Ye Haisheng's confession at the police station that involved Yang Wendao and questioned Yang. Yang categorically denied it, saying that he had never engaged in political activities. Then he said that in the summer of the 21st year, he was introduced by a friend and once served as a senator of the 55th Army. At that time, the military headquarters was stationed in Baotou, but he was in Shanghai. He resigned after less than two months in office. As for the Tongren and Tongyi associations he founded, they were all for charitable purposes. Tongyi had been dissolved due to financial difficulties. He never knew Xie Chunji, who opened room number nine at the Yuegong Hotel, and had never been to Yuegong, etc. When questioned, Zhou Sherong admitted that he was a member of Tongyi and said that Xie Chunji was also introduced by him to join Tongyi last October. When he confessed to being arrested this time, he burst into tears and insisted that he had been framed. Ye Haisheng, who was standing shoulder to shoulder with Zhou, was also in tears,

sobbing and crying.

Regarding the various situations confessed at the police station, he said that none of them were sincere. They were all words of agreement. Therefore, among the names mentioned, there were not a few who did not exist. At that time, he only wanted to make up the numbers and did not hesitate to fabricate them. When Judge Xiao questioned this, he believed that it was necessary to send Yang Wendao's palm print and the rust found in the books found in Yang's home to the Forensic Medicine Research Institute for identification. It was also necessary to check and retrieve a certain case file from the Jiangsu Higher Court. Therefore, he decided to adjourn the hearing. The three defendants, Yang, Ye, and Zhou, were still taken back to the police station for detention.

American's Car Kills Chinese Man - American Court Impartially Rules - Defendant Reiman Compensates in Chinese Currency to Close the Case 138

On the night of April 17th of this year, a small cart driver named Chen was pushing a cart on Haig Road when he was hit and injured by a car driven by an American named Reiman. He later died in the hospital. Subsequently, Chen's wife filed a lawsuit in the US Court in China and demanded compensation of US$10,000 for the loss. The case was finalized on the 4th by Chief Judge Hillmik. Because Chen was pushing the cart on the left side of the road in accordance with the regulations at the time, and the defendant's car was driving on the right side of the road, it could be seen regardless of the darkness of the night, but it still hit his small cart and injured him. The negligence cannot be shirked, so the defendant was ordered to compensate Chen's wife with 2,160 yuan in Chinese currency to close the case.

French Concession Police Department - Vehicle Traffic Rules 140

The French Concession Police Department, in view of the increased traffic in the concession, has studied various plans to avoid congestion at intersections and to facilitate traffic on major roads and cross streets, while ensuring the safety of pedestrians and the general public. The plan has been adopted and is now being implemented. Handcarts, small carts, and rickshaws are not allowed to travel on the following roads except for loading and unloading goods: Avenue Petain, Avenue Sieyes - from Avenue Petain to Avenue Terasse, Route Paul Henry from Avenue Massenet to Avenue Albert, Avenue du Parc from Avenue Dubail to Avenue Conty. If you want to load and unload goods on the above-mentioned roads, the vehicles should come from the cross street nearest to the destination, and must leave from the nearest cross street. All vehicles must park along the left side of the sidewalk according to the direction of travel, without obstructing traffic. Currently, all vehicles are not allowed to park at street corners or in areas listed on the police notice. Furthermore, in order to protect the sleep of residents in the concession, drivers of motor vehicles must not honk their horns indiscriminately at night, especially not to honk various horns at the same time.

Jianghai Customs Ordered to Prohibit Export of Waste Fluff - Representatives of Flying Flower Industry Petition in Beijing 141

Zhu Changnian, Superintendent of Jianghai Customs, and Ba Runsen, Tax Commissioner, jointly issued Notice No. 1536 yesterday, stating that they had received an order from the Ministry of Finance prohibiting the export of all waste fluff to foreign countries and ordering them to comply with it. Accordingly, they should comply with it and notify all merchants. This is a special announcement.

The Jianghai Customs was ordered by the Ministry of Finance to prohibit the export of waste fluff, mistakenly prohibiting the export of "flying flower" samples, causing great panic in the flying flower industry. Waste fluff is commonly known as old cotton wadding, also known as old broken fluff, which is removed from old cotton quilts and old cotton clothes. The customs export tariff lists it as 185. The various flying flower scraps produced by the spinning mills that cannot be spun, which are usually exported in large quantities, are worth 10 million yuan in national currency annually. The customs export tariff lists it as No. 175. The two are completely different. However, yesterday and today, the flying flowers declared for export were rejected by the customs. Therefore, the Shanghai Flying Flower Industry Association held an emergency meeting and sent representatives Xie Zhongle and Bao Guoliang to Beijing by night train last night to petition the Ministries of Finance and Industry, and to submit samples of flying flowers and waste fluff to explain the truth, so that flying flowers would not be subject to the same prohibition on export as waste fluff.

Rental Books and Garbage Cans - Petitioning the Municipal Government to Prohibit Sales - Expression of the Real Estate Industry Association 142

Landlords in Nanshi and Zhabei collect rent from tenants and must use the Anqing Bureau's rental books. Because the transportation, investigation, printing, and announcement costs were very high, it had to add subsidies in addition to the cost. The Real Estate Industry Association of this city, because this rental book has been issued for nearly four years, the Public Security Bureau's stored rental books should have been sold out. In addition, the Public Security and Health Bureaus stipulated that landlords should set up one garbage can per household, and those with two or more households within one dou must also have two or more garbage cans. Unexpectedly, after nearly a year, this garbage can had to be replaced again. The Maritime Department of the General Tax Office of Jianghai Customs has set up two light buoys at Lujiazui in the Huangpu River. It has issued Notice No. 1087, stating that the Jianghai Customs has set up two light buoys at Lujiazui in the Huangpu River to facilitate navigation. The setting situation and date are listed below for the information of all navigation merchants. Announcement: (1) Light buoy name: The two buoys are named Lujiazui Beach Buoy. (2) Light buoy shape: The two buoys are cone-shaped light buoys, painted black, each with a red fixed light. (3) Light buoy function: The two buoys are used to indicate the edge of the beach outside Lujiazui. (4) Light buoy position: The location of the two buoys is 18 feet below the lowest water level. Their positions are as follows: A. Lower buoy location: 41 degrees from the Jianghai Customs clock tower, 2,350 feet away. B. Upper buoy location: 47.5 degrees from the Jianghai Customs clock tower, 1,700 feet away. (5) Setting date: Estimated around August 7th of this year, no further announcements will be made at that time. (6) Relevant nautical chart: Republic of China Navy Hydrographic Chart Nos. 505 and 509, Maritime Department Surveyor Kanai.

The City Will Have a Large-Scale Tuberculosis X-Ray Group Examination - Held Every Tuesday and Saturday - Register at This Museum 149

According to the latest regulations on tuberculosis prevention, it is most effective to detect unconscious and latent pulmonary tuberculosis early in people who consider themselves healthy and to treat them before the disease develops. However, the symptoms of early-stage pulmonary tuberculosis are very subtle and difficult to distinguish. It is difficult to obtain an accurate diagnosis without X-ray examination. Therefore, many cases of delayed diagnosis have occurred. Dr. Ding Huikang, director of the Hongqiao Sanatorium in this port, has specially explored the latest X-ray group examination methods in various countries. Starting next week, examinations will be held at the Branch Hospital at 4 Daxi Road every Tuesday and Saturday morning. From now on, all groups or individuals only need to purchase an examination certificate from the museum. Each person only needs to pay one yuan and go to the registered time for examination. This examination is the first of its kind in our country and is of great benefit to the health of citizens.

The watermelons filled the harbor. Nearby sampans came forward to help rescue them. Five people were rescued on the spot, but Jin Yuanchang drifted outward with the current and was unable to be rescued in time, resulting in a tragic drowning. The body has not yet been recovered. According to the boat gang, the current was so rapid at the time that the person had been washed into the sea, so it was not easy to find the body. Moreover, one or two people are bound to suffer a disaster every summer in Wenzaobang. Jin Yuanchang is the first person this year.

Substituting Morphine Injections: Sentenced to Seven Years 163

Li Zhaokang and Qiu Zhenting, Chinese detectives of the Huishan Patrol House, discovered that someone was privately giving morphine injections for profit in House No. 7, Sanguantang Lane, Huaji Road. At 8:40 PM the day before yesterday, they secretly went with the Western detectives and arrested Wu San, a native of Tongzhou, who was administering the injections, along with his accomplice Xu Jiamo, as well as opium addicts who were injecting morphine to relieve their cravings, Zhang Zutao, Zhang Mincai, Mao Zhonghai, Li Jinbao, and others, as well as 33 small packets of morphine, three needles, a candle, and dozens of copper coins. All were taken to the Patrol House and detained. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Special District Court. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, stated that Wu San confessed at the Patrol House that the principal offender was a Chinese officer who had been dismissed from his post, No. 3174. It was found that Zhang Zutao and Li Jinbao were repeat offenders and incorrigible. Please punish them severely. Following this, the Chinese and Western detectives reported the details of the case, and the evidence was presented for inspection. Judge Zhong Qing questioned each defendant clearly and sentenced Wu San to seven years in prison, Xu Jiamo to three years, Zhang Zutao and Zhang Mincai to two years each, Mao Zhonghai and Li Jinbao were repeat offenders (who should be sentenced to death according to law) each reduced to seven years in prison. Before the execution, they were sent to a smoking cessation hospital for a period of no more than one month and ordered to quit. The evidence was confiscated as per the list.

Two Men and Women Throw Themselves into River, Liu Zhengxing Accused, Patrol House Believes There is Suspicion of Incitement, but Ding Huiyun Claims She Voluntarily Threw Herself into the River 165

Liu Xilin, a native of Changzhou, works as a waiter at the Baolong Hospital on Baker Road. His son, Liu Zhengxing, 23 years old this year, is an apprentice at the Meizuishi 洋行 on Jiujiang Road, No. 211. He married three years ago. Ding Shunlin, a cook at Baolong Hospital and a native of Changzhou, and Liu are both from the same hometown and colleagues, so the two are very close. Ding's family lives at No. 71, Dongsiwen Lane, Datong Road. He has a daughter named Huiyun, 20 years old this year, who is not yet engaged. In May of the year before last, Liu Zhengxing visited Ding's house and developed a relationship with Ding Huiyun out of friendship. The two were deeply in love and made a marriage agreement, but Liu already had a wife, so the future was inevitably hindered. Ding Shunlin's position was that his daughter could not marry him unless Liu divorced his wife. Liu then proceeded with the divorce proceedings, but because his wife demanded a thousand gold pieces in alimony, Liu was unable to afford this huge amount, so it was not completed. Recently, the aunt of Ding's daughter acted as an intermediary for her daughter, the other party being a middle-aged man in his thirties and a widower. The daughter of course objected, but the family proceeded urgently, and Ding Shunlin had no intention of allowing Liu to meet his daughter again. At about 8 PM the night before last, when it was raining heavily, Liu Zhengxing suddenly came to Ding's house and invited the woman out to talk. The woman then went out with him. They first wandered around the entrance of the Xihai Grand Theatre for more than an hour, and then braved the rain to go to the Bund Park. When people were unprepared, they threw themselves into the river together. Fortunately, gardener No. 36, No. 82, and Chinese police officer No. 952 heard the alarm and rushed to rescue the two and sent them to Renji Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, it was still early, and they were both saved. Subsequently, after investigation by Chief Inspector Jiang Shangpei and Bao Detective Jin Deshun of the General Patrol House, it was believed that Liu Zhengxing had incited suicide. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special District Court. Wang Yaotang, a lawyer from the Patrol House, prosecuted him in accordance with Articles 275-1 and 2 of the Criminal Law. Quan You Ding said that it was not Liu who asked me to die with him, but that I saw Liu throw himself into the river, and I thought that there was no fun in living in the world, so I followed him into the river. After Feng Shide, the judge, finished questioning the Chinese police and Liu Zhengxing, he ordered the verdict to be announced next Monday, and Liu was allowed to post bail on call.

Recently Published New Books: Two New Books by Jia He 166

Guangxia Bookstore, No. 528, 5th Floor, No. 128 Bowuyuan Road, recently published two new books by Mr. Jia He: "The Military, Political Parties, and Zaibatsu of Japan" and "Biography of Saigo Takamori." Le Zhenbao and Others Sued for Embezzlement Case Concluded, Sentencing on the 12th Morning 167

The Shanghai Foreign Goods Commercial Association on East Xinqiao Street in the French Concession, jointly established by nine industry guilds, had its property managed by four directors: Le Zhenbao (owner of Taichang Linqi Store on Nanjing Road), Bei Runsheng (former manager of Ruikang Paint Company), Zhang Lanping (current manager of Ruikang Paint Company), and Xi Gengrong (manager of Hengli Bank). The Xiyanliao Industry Association of this city was also one of the guilds under the former association. Recently, it was discovered that the four individuals in charge of the property, Le, Bei, Zhang, and Xi, had engaged in acts such as abusing their authority, embezzling property, and destroying evidence. After deliberation by the Fourth Plenary Session of all representatives of the said industry association and the 18th executive and supervisory meeting, Shou Shangjie was unanimously elected as the agent, who then retained lawyers Zhang Shizhao and Chao Kun to file a lawsuit with the Criminal Division of the Second Special Court, accusing Le Zhenbao, Bei Runsheng, Zhang Lanping, Xi Gengrong, and the other four individuals of concealing evidence, breach of trust and embezzlement, and requesting a legal trial. According to the intent of the lawsuit, there were sixteen businesses in the Xiyanliao industry that were affiliated with the Jiuye Gongsuo, or the Shanghai Foreign Goods Commercial Association, initiated by the defendants. At that time, during the European War, the pigment business was unusually prosperous, and the funds collected were substantial. The intention was to use these funds to build a guild hall when the industry flourished in the future. However, the Jiuye Gongsuo was originally formed by the merger of nine businesses, and the Xiyanliao industry formally established its own industry association in the 19th year of the Republic. Therefore, after negotiations, the association separated the sixteen businesses affiliated with the Jiuye Gongsuo. Regarding the related funds previously contributed by the industry, negotiations were also conducted to transfer them. After two reconciliations, an agreement was reached. Finally, the Foreign Goods Commercial Association would enjoy a monthly subsidy of 300 yuan from the Xiyanliao industry fund to cover its routine expenses. This agreement was mediated by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and filed with the Social Affairs Bureau, treating it as a collective agreement. After more than a year of fulfillment, Le Zhenbao and others suddenly changed the name of the Foreign Goods Commercial Association to the Renyi Shanhui (Benevolence, Righteousness, and Charity Association) and transferred the entire public property, under the guise of charity. At the same time, they refused to pay the agreed-upon subsidy, leading to renewed disputes. The association believed that the property rights and obligations with the Foreign Goods Commercial Association still existed, and based on the subject of the Xiyanliao industry in the agreement, like the whole egg, only the shell remains. It should transfer with the home of the egg, so the association has the need to recover it. Subsequently, the association discovered that the defendants were suspected of criminal acts in the disposal of public property, such as never reporting or disclosing annual accounts, repeatedly changing the name of the association's fund, covering the inscribed stone tablet with lime, and depositing all the proceeds into Xi Gengrong's own Hengli Bank for convenient use and investment in private enterprises. They believed that this constituted breach of trust and embezzlement and requested that the defendants be sentenced according to the law for their crimes. The case was heard twice by Judge Chen Shuoying, who ordered a postponement each time. This has already been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, the court continued the hearing. Plaintiff Ma Shangjie and his lawyers were present, and the defendants and their lawyers, Wu Linkun and Yan Yinwu, were also present. After the court questioned both parties, their statements were the same as before. After the questioning, the judge ordered opening statements. The lawyers on both sides gave eloquent arguments for over an hour. The court then declared the debate closed and scheduled sentencing for 8:00 AM on the 12th.

Overseas Cotton Prices Unanimously Plummet 181

Yesterday, the opening price of American cotton and news from Liverpool were unfavorable. Private estimates indicated an increase in supply. Liverpool and Southern sellers were active, and small-scale long positions were closed out. Prices for various months fell by six to ten points. Dealers and short sellers were the largest buyers, but resistance remained mediocre. Buyers were hesitant, awaiting the release of the government report. The current market price has fallen below the level before the July 8th report was published. The market situation remained sluggish at the close. As a result, spot prices fell by 20 points, and futures prices fell by 19 to 24 points. English cotton spot prices fell by 8 points, and futures prices fell by 16 to 19 points. Indian cotton initially fell due to selling by operators and closing out of long positions, with futures traders dumping their holdings. Later, prices rebounded slightly due to buying by dealers and hedging. Overall, Pingguoer fell by half a rupee, Aomula fell by 2.5 rupees, and Bailuoxi fell by 2.75 rupees. Original telegram from Zuo (dated the 4th).

According to a telegram from Mumbai dated the 5th, the opening price forecast was: Bailuoxi for July-August delivery at 224 rupees, down 2 rupees; Bailuoxi for April-May delivery at 212 rupees, down 1.75 rupees; Aomula for December-January delivery at 194 rupees, down 1.5 rupees.

Rangoon Cotton Exports: A telegram from Mumbai dated the 4th stated that the total amount of cotton exported from Rangoon in the past week was 139 tons, of which 99 tons went to Liverpool and 40 tons went to Hankou.

American Cotton Private Estimate: A telegram from New York dated the 4th stated that the Fox-Sick agency estimates this year's production percentage at 74.3%, with a total production of 12,511,000 bales.

Three Brands of Yarn and Cotton Continue to Fall: A telegram from Osaka dated the 5th stated that the price of three brands of futures yarn fell by 90 cents to 1.5 yuan, with the near month at 208.3 yuan and the far month at 201.6 yuan. The price of futures cotton fell by 65 cents to 1.05 yuan, with the near month at 67 yuan and the far month at 63.45 yuan.

Piece Goods: Eastern Cotton Cloth Also Fell Yesterday 182

Yesterday, due to the consistent weakness of yarn prices both domestically and internationally, sentiment was weak, and purchasing interest was greatly reduced. White cotton cloths such as fine cloth, fine twill, 84 cloth, and city cloth, among Eastern goods, each fell by 2.5 to 5 cents per piece. Dyed cloths such as Four Gentlemen serge and Zhigong fell by 7.5 cents per piece. Other patterned cloths and white cloths from local factories maintained their original prices. Transactions were not brisk, and the market was quiet. Single-thread serge and Zhigong from local factories, as well as mid-to-lower grade fine cloth and fine twill, were in relatively strong demand. Henan merchants showed the strongest purchasing interest, continuously buying hundreds of pieces of serge from factories such as Dacheng, Qingfeng, and Meiheng, as well as various brands of blue cloth and colored twill. Merchants from Hankou and Changsha were actively purchasing lower-grade fine cloth, fine twill, serge, Zhigong, crepe, and white flannel from local factories, as well as printed flannel and other goods. Merchants from Sichuan were also shipping over 200 pieces of floral flannel, bleached flannel, Shilin cloth, blue cloth, and Yuanslash cloth. Merchants from Guangdong and Yunnan had weak purchasing interest. Yesterday, merchants from Yunnan bought nearly 100 pieces of fine cloth, colored crepe, floral flannel, and Shilin cloth from Mufang. Wholesale stores on this street bought over 100 pieces of floral and plain Zhigong serge from the Lunchang factory, as well as small amounts of fine and coarse cloth.

Yin Feng Flannel Rises Very Rapidly 183

Yesterday, the textile market gradually became more active, and merchants were coming to market more often. The Japanese "6000" Yin Feng flannel was selling well with merchants from Changsha and Yu Rong. However, due to a lack of inventory in Shanghai, supply could not meet demand, and prices rose accordingly. Last week, 2.6-foot Yin Feng Yuan flannel sold for 77 cents, but now it has jumped to 83.5 cents net. Its price increase cannot be described as slow. If no new goods are received within ten days, the price should continue to rise. Judging from the recent trend of tight supply and strong sales, it could jump to 90 cents.

Grains: Japanese Merchants Continue to Purchase; Wheat Cash Price Rises, Futures Rebound 184

Yesterday, the wheat futures market opened with softness across all months, due to a sharp decline in foreign wheat prices. Market sentiment was uniformly moderate. However, outside speculators were largely selling, and inside shorts were taking advantage to cover their positions, so the decline in each month was only about one, two, four, or five cents. According to the current domestic situation, wheat prices are trending upwards. It is said that the wheat market in Wuxi has opened to 7.15 yuan, which is already higher than the price in Shanghai. Therefore, future trends may be difficult to reverse downwards in the short term. As for the cash wheat situation, Japanese merchants are continuously purchasing. It is said that brokers are mostly inspecting samples themselves, without going through the hands of experts. Medium-grade goods are fetching 55 to 60 cents, and special high-grade goods are at 4.7 to 4.8 yuan, with 2,000 to 3,000 bags traded. On the Shanghai factory side, due to weak arrivals, customers are pushing hard to sell high-grade goods, and the factory is finding it difficult to resist further. Special high-grade goods have reached 4.7 yuan, a significant increase of 10 cents compared to the previous day, while medium-grade goods are up by 5 to 6 cents. A total of 8,000 to 9,000 bags were opened in the general market.

Standard Flour Rebounds Slightly Due to Covering 185

Yesterday, after the flour market opened, all months remained quiet. Foreign wheat quoted one price, with Chicago falling by 80 to 90 cents and Canada falling by 1.1 to 1.2 yuan. When the opening price was quoted, sentiment for the current month was slightly more moderate due to the decline in foreign wheat, and the opening price was only 3.11 yuan, one cent away from the limit price. However, in subsequent trading sessions, the trend rebounded due to floating shorts covering, rising by 7.5 li, still within the limit price. The main reason is that actual sales have recently slowed down slightly, so many long positions have been disposed of. As for the months from September onwards, since foreign wheat only fell for one day, sentiment remained firm, and all stood at the limit price. Future trends will depend on foreign wheat prices.

Inexhaustible Supply, Rising Wind of Ke Xian 186

Yesterday, Ke Xian and Ke Hua rice remained active. In addition to merchants on this street and from the mainland, merchants from Sichuan and Guangzhou Ningbo were also very active, but the volume of sales was not as strong as in previous days. Coupled with the inexhaustible supply, domestic merchants were willing to sell. After the market price had risen for several days, more goods arrived from all directions, and the owners also wanted to sell as soon as possible to avoid being squeezed out by new goods. Therefore, the rising wind has been thwarted, and the market has become stable. If the sales path becomes strong again in the future, the market price may be able to gradually recover. A total of 3,450 bags of various Jiangxi rice, 1,000 bags each of Xiang Jing Sha rough rice, were opened for sale, with this street being the most active buyer. Merchants from Sichuan and Guangdong each bought 1,000 bags, while merchants from Ningbo and other places in the mainland only made small purchases.

Dongxin Japonica Rice Arrives Sparsely, Price Rises 187

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, shipments arrived from various merchants totaling 16 or 17 shipments, with a total of 3,200 to 3,300 dan. Sales on this street were even more sluggish. Merchants from Qinhuangdao bought only one hundred and ten bags, so the market situation showed a sign of softening. High-grade Houzao Japonica rice prices were reduced by nearly 10 cents, while medium-grade rice depreciated by a few cents. Good-quality Boda rice fell by one scale, while medium-grade rice fell by about two scales. Doyang Jian rice was scarce and barely managed to hold its price. Yinbian Yuan rice had no fluctuations. Yesterday, Xinchang factory shipped 40 shi of Dongxin rice. Due to continuous rain, supplies were occasionally cut off, and the price increased by 20 cents.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, more than ten shipments arrived from various merchants downstream. Sales of various types of goods on the market: Baijing Yang Du Bu Ke Jian were stagnant, while Yuan rice was scarce and still good. The market price of Baijing was slightly fatigued, by a few cents. Yang Du Bu Ke Jian were down by a few cents to nearly 10 cents, Bianyuan were slightly up. Boda rice had nothing to be ashamed of. Dongxin rice was scarce and unavailable in the market.

After the opening of soybean oil trading, there was much closing out of floating long positions, and the market and sentiment were both flat. Eleventh Olympic Games 1936

After Qualifying in the Pole Vault Preliminaries, Fu Baolu Was Eliminated in the Finals. Owens Sets Another New Record in the Long Jump and 200 Meters. Our National Soccer Team Will Play England Today. 196

(Berlin) The Olympic Games held the pole vault preliminary round at 10:30 am on the 5th. The qualifying standard was 3.80 meters. Our national athlete Fu Baolu cleared the bar on his second attempt, becoming the only Chinese athlete to participate in the finals. At the same time, in the discus preliminary round, only those who could exceed 44 meters were allowed to qualify. Our national athletes Guo Jie and Leng Peigen both failed to qualify and were eliminated. (Central News Agency, 5th)

(Berlin) Chinese pole vaulter Fu Baolu qualified in today's pole vault preliminary, clearing a standard height of 12 feet 6 inches. Leng Peigen and Guo Jie were eliminated in the discus preliminary, both failing to throw past the standard distance of 144 feet 4 inches. Chen Baoqiu withdrew from this competition. (Reuters, 5th) In today's Olympic soccer match, our country will play against the English team. The match will start at 4 pm Berlin time, which is around 11 pm Shanghai time. Unfortunately, our country will face the home of soccer in the first match. However, England's amateur soccer is not as strong as we imagined. At that time, our team's athletes will definitely give them a very fierce resistance. However, due to the time difference between Europe and Asia, it is not yet known whether the results of this match can be received tonight.

(Berlin) The Olympic pole vault finals were held at 4 pm on the 5th. Our national athlete Fu Baolu cleared 3.80 meters, but failed to clear 4 meters, and was eventually eliminated.

Owens Deserves the Title of "Flying Legs": Reconstructs the World Record in the Long Jump with a Score of 8.06 Meters 197

Central News Agency Special Correspondent, Berlin, 4th - The long jump final of the World Games was held at 4:30 PM this afternoon at the main stadium. The first place was again won by the American Negro, Owens. Second place went to Long (Germany), third to Tajima Naoto (Japan), fourth to Maffei (Italy), fifth to Cark (USA), and sixth to Leichum (Germany). The score was 8.06 meters, setting a new world record. (Note: The highest world record in the long jump was 7.98 meters, set by Japanese athlete Nambu Chuhei in 1931.)

Domei News Agency, Berlin, 4th - The results of the long jump final are as follows: (Note) The world record for the long jump is 7.98 meters, set by Nambu Chuhei (Japan) on October 27, 1931, in Tokyo, Japan. The Olympic record is 7.73 meters, set by Hamm of the United States in the 9th Games in 1928.

National News Agency, Berlin, August 4th - American star Owens is not only excellent in sprints but also excels in the long jump. After setting a new record in the 200 meters, his heroic spirit remains. This afternoon, he broke the World Games and world record in the long jump, displaying awe-inspiring power, to the amazement of the audience. The most exciting moment of the World Games this afternoon was Owens breaking the world record with a jump of 8.06 meters.

This morning, Owens had already set a record in the 200 meters at the Games. Riding the momentum of a hundred victories, his genius shines brightly, and he again set a world record in the long jump, truly deserving his reputation as a hero of his time.

The World Games long jump record was 7.87 meters, set by Owens in the preliminary round this morning. However, this record was not destined to last long, as the German Lange equaled this record with one jump. But Owens then improved upon his previous preliminary record, advancing it to 7.97 meters. However, the black star Owens still felt unsatisfied and wanted to go even further. So, he jumped again and achieved 8.06 meters, reaching the peak of perfection, deserving of all praise. Thus, Owens won another gold medal. The German Lange took second place with 7.87 meters, and the Japanese Tajima Naoto was third with 7.74 meters. The remaining three places went to the Italian Maffa, the German Leichum, and the American Clark. The top two had scores of 7.73 meters, while Clark had 7.67 meters.

American black star Owens (left) and Muto Cav (right)

Preliminary Football Matches: Japan Defeats Sweden; Germany Defeats Luxembourg 199

As a result, Germany won with a score of nine to zero.

Discus Final: American Athlete Sets Games Record; Top Two Places Are Both American Athletes 200

Central News Agency Special Correspondent, Berlin, 5th - The men's discus final of the World Games was held at 3:00 PM on the 5th. As a result, the first place went to Carpenter (USA), the second place to Dunn (USA), the third place to Oberweger (Italy), the fourth place to Sorlie (Norway), the fifth place to Schroeder (Germany), and the sixth place to Syllas (Greece). The score was 50.48 meters, setting a new Games record. (Note: The Games record was 49.48 meters, set by Anderson of Sweden.)

National News Agency, Berlin, August 5th - The top two places in the discus final both belong to the United States. The scores of the top three are as follows:

(Note) Carpenter's score breaks the Games record of 49.49 meters. The old record was set by Anderson of Sweden in Los Angeles in 1932, but it is still almost two meters short of Anderson's 52.42 meters.

National News Agency, Berlin, August 5th - Unfortunately, the weather on the fourth morning of the World Games was not "very Games-like." It was cold and rainy. After the discus qualifying round, the pole vault qualifying round had to be postponed. Thirty-three athletes participated in the discus qualifying round, and thirteen were able to exceed the standard distance of 44 meters. Many athletes were affected by the cold weather. The following athletes qualified: Suli of Norway, West Weising of Norway, Pigg of Sweden, Noir of France, Carpenter and Dunn and Wood of the US, Hitterwall of Sweden, Slute and Fritz of Germany, Silas of Greece, Oppai Vise of Italy, and Utpai of Austria. Rotary Cup: China Wins Over Germany 218

In the 7th International Rotary Cup Tennis Championship, China first played against Germany on the 1st of this month. China won both singles matches on the 2nd and 3rd. The first singles match and the first and second doubles matches were originally scheduled to continue on the 2nd, but due to continuous rainy days, they were only completed yesterday at the German Garden Association. As a result, China won all again. The overall result was five to zero, with China winning over Germany and advancing to the second week. If the weather and venue are suitable, the match against England will be decided at the Kangti Association on the 8th and 9th. The first week of the United States vs. Portugal and France vs. Japan will also be held on the 7th, 8th, and 9th respectively. The second week of the competition between the winning teams from the United States and Portugal and the winning teams from Japan and France will be held on the 11th, 12th, and 13th of this month. Therefore, the final date is still expected to follow the original scheduled dates of the 15th and 16th.

In the Issue of Women's Fitness, the Most Important Problem to Pay Attention to is Menstrual Regulation; Maintaining Regular Menstruation Leads to a Healthy and Beautiful Body; Taking Fotz’s Dang Gui Su Can Regulate Menstruation and Nourish Blood 221

A healthy mother is necessary for a healthy baby. This is why women's health should be the first priority. Women's health is based on menstruation. If there are pathological changes in menstruation, then normal health is lost, and this violates the principles of health.

Women's menstruation, with healthy eggs, is necessary for healthy embryos, and is related to human reproduction, which is of utmost importance. In the past, women were deeply secluded and did not connect with the world. Therefore, they did not know the times and were often stubborn. Liver disease was deep-seated, and exercise was neglected. Modern women have many social interactions, advocate liberation, and set foot in the market. The disadvantages of indulgence are becoming more profound, and menstrual diseases are becoming more obvious. Some are due to excessive labor in poor families, or due to family oppression and excessive restraint. Excessive games lead to wandering thoughts, and excessive worry leads to stagnation of qi. All of these factors can lead to menstrual diseases.

The way to regulate menstruation is to eliminate disease first. Those who suffer from diseases that lead to irregular menstruation should have their diseases treated, and then the menstrual disease will be cured naturally. This is the so-called etiological therapy. For example, excessive sorrow, or anger harming the liver, or poor relief, or abnormal fright, can cause qi and blood to merge and nerves to be affected, which is commonly known as neurasthenia. Blood follows the flow of qi, and when qi is sick, blood is sick. Traditional medicine says that heat comes before menstruation, and stagnation comes after. The reasoning is similar, but it should not be taken too literally. For example, if the internal organs are empty and menstruation drips continuously and frequently, it should not be judged as heat. Also, if there is internal heat, blood depletion, and slow and uneven menstrual flow, it should not be judged as cold. One must examine the combined symptoms. If the pulse is rapid and there is internal heat, dry lips and mouth, and aversion to heat and preference for cold, then there is heat. If the pulse is slow and cold, the tongue is pale and the mouth is neutral, and there is a preference for heat and aversion to cold, then there is cold. If menstruation is heavy in flow and bright in color, then there is excess blood. If there is little blood and the color is pale, then qi is stagnant and the abdomen is coagulated. If there is emptiness and pain during menstruation and one likes to press with their hands, then qi is deficient and blood is low. Those who suffer from this symptom should take "Foz’s Dang Gui Su" internally, which is a simple and effective treatment for the family. After taking it for several weeks, it will definitely regulate the menstrual cycle and restore healthy beauty.

Dang Gui is the root of Dang Gui, a material of the category , produced in various parts of the central part of our country. It is a sacred medicine for gynecology and can make qi and blood return to their respective places, hence the name. Shen Nong's Materia Medica and Li Shizhen's Compendium of Materia Medica both recognize Dang Gui as the only sacred product for nourishing blood, regulating menstruation, warming the palace, and pregnancy. Dr. Hillt, a German gynecological expert, studied Chinese medicine and used scientific methods to extract the effective ingredients of Dang Gui produced in China. After repeated animal experiments, all the results were amazing. Therefore, the Western medical community recognizes Dang Gui as a special medicine for gynecology, and many new doctors in our country also appreciate its use.

"Foz’s Dang Gui Su" is improved and prepared based on our country's ancient and proven prescriptions, Dang Gui San, Dang Gui Yin from Women's Good Prescription, Dang Gui powder from Must-Work Prescription, Dang Gui Pills from Universal Relief Prescription, Dang Gui Decoction from Sacred Blessing Prescription, etc. Therefore, it has a history of thousands of years of clinical experience, and our factory also selects domestic Dang Gui and uses a vacuum distiller to extract its essence with scientific methods for improvement and preparation. Its effect is indeed superior to foreign-made Dang Gui essence, and it is very convenient to take and carry.

According to a report by gynecological expert Dr. Ann: "Dang Gui Su" was administered to fourteen patients with dysmenorrhea and four patients with amenorrhea, all with satisfactory results. Those with dysmenorrhea experienced gradual relief from pain, and all other unpleasant symptoms were swept away. Those with amenorrhea had their menstrual flow restored to normal.
